A New Page in Post-War European History: Franco-Italian Agreement Signed

Urges Germany to Return to the League of Nations and Discuss Disarmament

Cooperation to Maintain Peace

(Rome) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval signed three important agreements and several additional protocols today. This is a major step forward in the post-World War I movement for universal peace. The three main agreements are as follows:

(1) Franco-Italian Colonial Agreement;

(2) Danube River Agreement, also concerning guaranteeing Austrian independence;

(3) European Peace Consultation Agreement;

The important signing ceremony was held at the Palazzo Venezia at 7 PM this evening. Mussolini, representing the Italian government, and Laval, representing the French government, signed first. Italian representative to the League of Nations, Sir Aloisi, Italian Foreign Minister Suvich, and French Ambassador to Italy de Chambrun also signed as witnesses. In addition, several documents were signed, aiming to create an atmosphere of peace in Europe. These documents explicitly state that France and Italy jointly invite Germany to return to the League of Nations to cooperate in maintaining peace.

The Associated Press learned from responsible sources that Britain and Germany will soon announce their acceptance of the treaty guaranteeing Austria's integrity. Mussolini and Laval shook hands and congratulated each other after signing, showing their warm feelings. France and Italy also agreed to reopen disarmament negotiations based on the Italian memorandum of January 19, 1934, to resolve issues such as Germany's demand for military equality, Germany's return to the League of Nations, and the determination of Germany's disarmament limits. This agreement has now been sent to the Berlin authorities. Diplomatic circles here say that Germany supports this plan. (Seventh day Kuomin News)

(Rome) French Foreign Minister Laval departed from Rome for Paris this afternoon. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Suvich, Chairman of the League of Nations Saar Committee Aloisi, and other important Italian figures all personally saw him off. Crowds of onlookers lined the streets, cheering loudly. Soldiers were stationed along the route to provide strict protection. Traffic was cut off at the train station, and a military band played music outside the platform. The farewell scene between the French Foreign Minister and the Italian Prime Minister was extremely friendly, demonstrating the friendship between France and Italy. Neither France nor Italy commented on the disarmament provisions in the agreement, but it is said that the provisions mentioned Germany. According to sources in Paris, the provisions mention Germany's return to the League of Nations under certain cautionary conditions after rearming. (Eighth day Reuters dispatch)

France and Italy Congratulate Each Other on Success

Rome: Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval signed an agreement last night on Austria's independence and Italy's acquisition of concessions in North Africa. This is the greatest success of general European peace efforts since the Great War. The signing took place at the Palazzo Venezia, with three main agreements signed: a diplomatic protocol, an agreement on colonial affairs, an agreement on the Danube region and guaranteeing Austria's independence, and an agreement on implementing consultation policies for the sake of European peace. In addition, there are several documents aimed at creating an atmosphere of peace among European countries. Judging from appearances, a political agreement may be completed with the assistance of the Bank of France to the Italian Bank.

After signing the agreement, Laval declared to the press that neither country had sacrificed important interests and that they had decided to discuss everything in detail so that the agreement could become a reality. Their policy is to participate on the basis of moral equality, with the sole purpose of contributing possible opportunities for the cause of peace organization to all governments. He firmly believes that their appeal will be answered. After Laval's speech, Mussolini said that they should not think that everything has been successful and must still cultivate the friendship between the two countries, which is formed by a common glorious civilization and the major trials of recent times. Mussolini then praised Laval, saying that the two had undergone the same political experiences, so they understood each other. Finally, he said that the year of reckless judgment has now begun with the joyful signing of the treaty.

Last night, the authorities issued a brief communique, which did not contain the contents of the agreement, nor did it mention the issue of limiting armaments. However, limiting armaments must be part of the treaty, and it is also reported that France intends to invite Germany to return to the League of Nations, which must be involved in one of the protocols. There was no hostility towards Germany in the text, nor was it mentioned that Germany's rearmament was illegal.

Abyssinia is the focus of the colonial agreement. Italy has obtained several concessions under this agreement. Some sources say that France has accepted Italy's application, allowing Italy to act freely in Abyssinian commercial and colonial affairs, but this has not been officially confirmed and does not seem to be included in the text.

The British and French governments have recently urged the Italian government to seek a peaceful resolution to the Ualual dispute with Abyssinia. Relations between Italy and Abyssinia seem to have improved somewhat in recent days.

The concessions obtained by Italy under the colonial agreement are as follows:

(1) Italians in Tunis retain their Italian nationality for two generations; (2) Italy will obtain a strip of land north of the Tibesti Massif, 800 miles long and 100 miles wide;

(3) Italy will obtain the land of Belmaté Blanc in French Somaliland, excluding the port of Djibouti. Italy may purchase between 2,000 and 3,000 shares of the Djibouti-Addis Ababa railway.

France is very pleased with the success of the Rome Agreement. Paris now feels that Germany will not stay out of it, and the progress that France and Italy have made towards a disarmament agreement is better than initially expected. France has clearly accommodated Italy's position, which will make Laval's upcoming trip to London even more important.

German political circles have not yet commented on the Franco-Italian agreement. According to a Reuters dispatch from Berlin, the German government is concentrating on matters related to the Saar plebiscite, so it seems unlikely that it will express an opinion before next week. (Eighth day Reuters dispatch)

Communique After Signing

(Rome) After the official signing of the Franco-Italian agreement, the following communique was issued to the press at 8:30 PM: (As a result of the Franco-Italian talks held by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval, several agreements have been signed concerning the interests of the two countries in Africa and declaring the consensus of the two governments on European issues. Mussolini and Laval jointly stated that it is necessary to obtain a multi-faceted understanding on the issue of Central Europe. The two governments fully agree and believe that the proposals already adopted on the issue of Central Europe should be submitted to the relevant countries for review as soon as possible. On the one hand, while waiting for the signing of such a multi-faceted agreement, on the other hand, France and Italy will jointly review various measures to deal with the current situation in the spirit of this understanding.) (Seventh day Havas dispatch)

German Diplomatic Circles Surprised

(Berlin) The sudden turn of events in the Rome talks and the establishment of a broad agreement between France and Italy have surprised diplomatic circles here. Although the diplomatic authorities here refused to take any position before the official announcement of the Franco-Italian agreement, they could not help but reveal their suspicion of the agreement. The reason for their deep suspicion is the fear that Germany's diplomatic policy after the Saar plebiscite will be greatly hindered by the rapprochement between France and Italy, and that the rapprochement between France and Italy will inevitably greatly undermine the movement to revise the peace treaty. The German General Review commented on the non-interference in Austria's internal affairs, saying that the German people will never forget the important event of other countries interfering in internal affairs, namely the drafting of the Treaty of Versailles, which prohibited the merger of Austria and Germany. The Berlin Daily said that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has repeatedly expressed his support for revising the peace treaty to his people. Mussolini's ability to win people's hearts is mostly due to this spirit and influence. However, the so-called agreement to ensure the security of Central Europe runs counter to the spirit of treaty revision.

(Berlin) Although only one of the four recently concluded Italo-French agreements has been made public, its content has been largely speculated and known by the outside world, and various governments can express their official attitudes. According to the German Foreign Policy Review, as far as Europe is concerned, this agreement must be divided into two, namely the Franco-Italian Consultative Agreement and the Central European Non-Interference Agreement. Among them, only the Franco-Italian Consultative Agreement is an accomplished fact, because Mr. Mussolini has changed the responsibility for maintaining the independence of Austria from Italy alone to be shared by France. As for the Central European Agreement, not only France and Italy are promoting its realization, but all Central European countries are involved, especially the major powers, because this is not only a problem of Austria, but a problem of the entire Danube region. This involves the relationship between Hungary and the Little Entente countries and the relationship between Yugoslavia and Italy. Although the progress of Franco-Italian relations is a major key to the European situation, which cannot be ignored, there are still many problems to be solved urgently, especially economic problems. (Eighth day Minguo News)

Simon Expresses Gratification

(London) British Foreign Secretary Simon, after returning to London with his wife last night, said to people, (I am very gratified to hear of the success of the Rome Agreement. Although I have not been able to see its official full text, the conclusion of this agreement is indeed a good thing.) Simon also said, (French Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval can make a trip to London within the month as agreed.) (Eighth day Kuomin News)

(Rome) British Ambassador to Italy Sir Drummond met with French Foreign Minister Laval this afternoon. After the Franco-Italian agreement was signed, Drummond was received by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. (Seventh day Havas dispatch)

Hungary's Unease

Budapest: Hungary has been uneasy about the talks on Austrian independence held in Rome. According to government sources, Hungarian public opinion does not approve of the government's involvement in guaranteeing Austria's current borders, because the Burgenland region of Austria was originally Hungarian territory, but was later ceded to Austria after the Treaty of Trianon was concluded. If Hungary now participates in guaranteeing Austria's current territory, it would be tantamount to unconditionally abandoning that land. Hungary is dissatisfied with the current borders of Czechoslovakia and Romania, but can submit a reservation to Yugoslavia and temporarily agree to it. (Seventh day Kuomin News)

United States Expresses Deep Interest

(Washington) The conclusion of the Rome Agreement between France and Italy, especially the conclusion of the protocol on the issue of German armaments, has deeply impressed the State Department. Both the White House and the State Department believe that the time for the revival of the disarmament conference is not far off. US Minister to Switzerland Wilson is scheduled to return to Europe on January 10 with President Roosevelt's instructions. General opinion here believes that the site of the disarmament conference has been cleared, making it easy for Germany to rejoin the disarmament conference. In the next disarmament talks, the United States may be very active. President Roosevelt's 1933 proposal to strictly define the aggressor nation and his proposal last year to revise the principle of freedom of the seas will probably be re-presented. If there is an opportunity to conclude an agreement on limiting armaments, there must be detailed discussions in the first meeting in Geneva this year. (Seventh day Havas dispatch)

Austrian Government Denies Attempted Assassination of Deputy Prime Minister

(Vienna) The government today denied the Communist Party's plot to assassinate Deputy Prime Minister and Commander-in-Chief of the Internal Security Forces, Prince Starhemberg. (Eighth day Kuomin News)

Hitler Reorganizes Guards to Deal with Internal Enemies

(Berlin) According to reliable sources, German leader Hitler is secretly reorganizing his elite Black Shirt Guards, forming the first regiment with 20,000 people. The weaponry they use is more sophisticated than that of the existing Black Shirt Guards. It is said that the purpose of this move is to deal with internal enemies, which is a prelude to reducing the Black Shirt Guards. (Seventh day Reuters dispatch)

Saar Bans Assemblies

Saarbrücken: The Saar Plebiscite Commission, after consulting with the Governing Commission, issued an order today prohibiting people from holding assemblies from the 10th of this month until the day the vote is announced. All public and private organizations in the region must comply with this ban, except for theaters and cinemas. (Seventh day Kuomin News)

(Berlin) Several newspapers here are very resentful of the Saar Plebiscite Commission's cancellation of the votes cast yesterday. The reason for the invalidation is that the voters performed the Hitler salute when voting and did not use black pencils to write, violating the voting regulations. The voters yesterday were civil servants, because they will be constrained by their duties during the general vote on the 13th and will not be able to vote. (Eighth day Kuomin News)

Saarbrücken: Administrative officials, police, and railway workers in the Saar region must continue to work on the 13th, that is, the day of the plebiscite. Therefore, the Plebiscite Commission specially set up a polling station for them to vote in advance today. However, the number of voters seems to be quite small. As of now, only 201 out of 2,200 voters in Saarbrücken have voted. Civil servants who cannot vote today may still vote tomorrow or on the 13th. (Seventh day Havas dispatch)

5,000 Students Attack Red Shirt Headquarters: Religious Disputes in Mexico

Mexico: The anti-religious movement has disrupted Mexico's security for several years, and today the situation is heating up again. 5,000 students suddenly attacked the headquarters of the Red Shirts, driving out the anti-Catholic Red Shirt members and shooting five Red Shirt members. Angry students threw bricks at the headquarters, smashing doors, windows, and glass. It is said that the Red Shirts fired first, and the two sides exchanged fire for about 15 minutes before the Red Shirts surrendered. After the students broke in, they destroyed everything in the room. Police and fire trucks arrived at the scene after the incident to suppress the students and disperse them. Fortunately, there were no deaths or injuries. About a dozen students were arrested, and the rest of the students marched in formation through the streets, shouting slogans against the government's anti-religious policies. (Seventh day Kuomin News)

Iran-Iraq Border Dispute Placed on League of Nations Agenda

Iranian Foreign Minister Arrives in Geneva

(Geneva) Iranian Foreign Minister Kazemi has arrived here today to participate in the League of Nations meeting to discuss the border incident between Iran and Iraq. Last November, the Iraqi government sent a letter to the League of Nations, stating that Iran had repeatedly violated the border and requesting that the League of Nations Council handle it. The case was immediately placed on the agenda of this session of the Council. (Eighth day Havas dispatch)

Peruvian Rebellion Crushed

Lima, Peru: A hundred people attacked the barracks of Cayma, and after several hours of fierce fighting, the rebellion was finally crushed. Seven rebels and one soldier died. The rebels launched a second attack, but fortunately the central army stood firm and did not retreat, so they were not successful. After the rebels were driven away a second time, the soldiers in the barracks counterattacked and charged forward, and the rebels fled into the mountains. (Seventh day Guomin News)

Collision of Soviet Express Trains

Sixteen Dead, Sixty-Seven Injured

Negligence Caused the Accident

One Theory Points to Sabotage

(Moscow) Yesterday, two special express trains collided on the Moscow-Leningrad railway line, resulting in sixteen deaths and sixty-seven injuries. It is reported that the two trains were traveling on the same track. The leading train suffered minor mechanical damage, reducing its speed. The driver of the following train failed to heed the stop signal and continued as usual, causing it to collide with the rear of the leading train. Three carriages of the leading train caught fire and were destroyed. Authorities are now investigating to determine responsibility. The driver and his assistant on the following train, as well as three railway employees, have been detained. If negligence is proven, they will be executed by firing squad. (Reuters, 8th)

(Paris) According to the Petit Parisien newspaper, a Moscow dispatch states that two express trains on the Moscow main line collided 135 miles from Leningrad. Several carriages were reduced to wreckage, and three were consumed by fire. Casualties were numerous. (Reuters, 8th)

(Paris) According to a Berlin telegram printed in Le Matin, twenty bodies have been recovered from the wreckage of the train accident on the Moscow-Leningrad railway. In addition, there are many injured. It is reported that the accident was the result of sabotage, and several railway employees have been arrested. (Havas, 8th)

Retrial of Lindbergh Kidnapping Case: Nanny's Testimony

Admits to Informing Boyfriend of Household Activities

Hauptmann's Face Turns Ashen in Court

Flemington: The retrial of the Lindbergh kidnapping case continued today. Defendant Hauptmann turned gray when Betty Gow arrived to testify about the circumstances of the Lindbergh baby's disappearance. The prosecutor presented the witness with a baby garment found near Lindbergh's body. Gow choked and said, "I think I made this." She continued, "On the night of March 1, 1932, at 10 p.m., I entered the nursery. Fearing to wake the child, I did not turn on the light, but felt the crib in the dark. It was empty. Knowing something was wrong, I rushed out to tell Colonel Lindbergh. He ran upstairs and called to his wife, 'Anne, they have stolen our child!' Lindbergh then grabbed a gun and rushed outside, while the women of the house sat silently inside, waiting," she said. At this point, the defendant's lawyer cross-examined Gow about her boyfriend. Gow admitted that she was friends with a young man, one of whom was named Red Johnson, who is now in Norway, and stated that New Jersey provided her expenses, asking her to come to the United States from Norway to testify at Hauptmann's trial and give her 650 dollars, and Gow confessed that she had told Red Johnson about the Lindbergh family's actions. The defendant's lawyer asked if she had heard the dog bark that night. Gow replied that she had not, and that the actions of the cook's wife, Wetley, did not raise the dog's suspicions. The defendant's lawyer continued to cross-examine, hoping to prove that although the kidnapping was not carried out by the Lindbergh family, the plan may have been drawn up in the Lindbergh household. At the end of the cross-examination, Gow broke down and cried, but quickly composed herself, wiped away her tears, and powdered her face. (Reuters, 7th)

Flemington: When questioned by reporters today about the ladder outside the Lindbergh baby's bedroom window, Hauptmann, accused of kidnapping and murdering the Lindbergh baby, replied that if he had placed the ladder, he would be a very bad carpenter. Prosecutor Hawke claimed that the authorities would prove that the footprints under the bedroom window were made by Hauptmann because two soldiers wearing size nine shoes had placed their feet in these footprints and found them to be quite suitable. It is known that Hauptmann also wears size nine shoes. (Reuters, 8th)

U.S. Political Parties Criticize New Budget Proposal

Revenue Insufficient to Cover Expenditures Hinders Recovery

Large Increase in National Debt Causes Concern

(Washington) Both the Democratic and Republican parties have expressed concern over the large increase in the national debt in their criticisms of the budget proposal submitted to Congress by President Roosevelt today. Expenditures for the fiscal year beginning July 1 will total $8,520,000,000, while revenue is estimated at only $3,992,000,000. Congressman Taber, a Republican member of the Appropriations Committee, stated today that if this continues, we will only prevent recovery. Senator McNary, the Republican leader, stated that it was regrettable that the authorities had failed to balance the budget, but that relief for the unemployed was necessary. Democratic Senator Smith stated that recovery will not be achieved until we find a way to restore foreign trade. Other critics have expressed the intention of Congress to put a check on the huge expenditures proposed by President Roosevelt. Some also said that the financial community will become even more confused and that the burden on taxpayers will become increasingly heavy in the future. (Reuters, 7th)

(New York) A clause in the National Industrial Recovery Act states that the President may prohibit the transportation of petroleum produced in excess of the maximum limit permitted by the government, with violators subject to fines or imprisonment. The Federal Supreme Court has recently declared this clause invalid. In addition, there are other issues under consideration by the court. It seems certain that the court will uphold the cancellation of the clause in debt contracts requiring payment in cash. (Havas, 7th)

Sharp Fall in Silver Prices in Bombay

Bombay: News of President Roosevelt's budget message to Congress from Washington has had a major impact on the Bombay silver market. Today, the spot price opened at Rs. 64.07, twelve annas lower than the closing price on Sunday. Later, it was still ten annas, and the price fell to Rs. 63.13. However, sentiment turned strong in the afternoon, and the price rebounded to Rs. 64.04, seven annas higher than the morning closing price. It then rose another anna at 5:30 p.m. Today's sharp fall in silver prices was caused by short-sellers interpreting the Washington news as a harbinger of a major reduction in the silver coinage tax in 1936. Speculators who had bought too much panicked and closed their positions, believing it to be a sign that the U.S. silver purchase program in 1935 would become calmer. (Reuters, 8th)

Movement of Far East Red Army

Manchouli: Recently, there have been frequent delays on the Siberian Railway connecting to Manchouli due to the large-scale movement of the Red Army between Buragoveshchensk and Vladivostok, which is causing delays due to busy transport. (Dentsu, 8th)

Changgang, New Director of the Guandong Bureau, Discusses Policy Towards the Puppet State

Actively Implementing Economic Controls

President of South Manchuria Railway to Remain Temporarily

Pu Yi Scheduled to Visit Tokyo in April

(Tokyo) Changgang Longyilang, the newly appointed Director-General of the Guandong Bureau, departed from Tokyo Station at 9:00 a.m. today for Manchuria via Korea. Changgang made the following remarks on the train: "The policy towards Manchuria will be carried out according to established guidelines. I intend to serve under the command of the new South Manchuria ambassador with all sincerity. My task is to handle the administration of the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway's affiliated lands. I have no intention of changing personnel. I will proceed after taking office, based on the principle of placing people according to their talents. The rumor of replacing the President and Vice President of the South Manchuria Railway is completely false. There are no problems with the current South Manchuria Railway, so this kind of rumor is a bit premature. As for the Japan-Manchuria Economic Conference, I intend to study it after gathering opinions from various foreign regions." (Dentsu, 8th)

(Changchun) Pu Yi is scheduled to formally visit Japan on April 1. (Domei, 7th)

Japanese Finance Minister Explains Controlled Investment in Manchuria

(Tokyo) Finance Minister Takahashi explained at the cabinet meeting on the 8th the situation of Japan's exports and imports to Manchuria within Showa 9 (1934), the status of investments in Manchuria, and other related matters, drawing the attention of the cabinet members. The Finance Minister's proposal showed a desire to control future investments in Manchuria. The details of his explanation are recorded on the left:

"In Showa 9, Japan's foreign trade achieved its best results, with increases in both imports and exports, and a considerable trend towards balancing overseas receipts and payments with freight and other non-trade receipts. This is commendable for Japanese trade. What I want to draw to the attention of the cabinet members now is that the total amount of investment in Manchuria in Showa 9 has reached a huge sum of 140 million yuan. However, this amount of investment will absolutely not cause unease in the financial community, because the investment in (Manchukuo) will be recovered in the future. However, in future investments, it seems that control is necessary. Originally, Manchuria is also a foreign country, and it should not be treated the same as investing in the mainland, and it is directly related to the exchange rate. Especially since the recent Sino-Soviet Railway negotiations are about to be concluded, we must also pay attention to increasing capital. There are also fears that Japanese capital invested in (Manchukuo) will escape elsewhere in the future. Therefore, when investing in Manchuria in the future, please fully consult with the Ministry of Finance and carefully discuss it before making a decision." (Domei, 8th)

U.S. Secretary of State and Treasury Secretary Discuss Silver Issue

U.S.-China Negotiations Underway; Easing Silver Purchases a Natural Result

(Washington) The Associated Press has learned from reliable sources that Secretary of State Hull and Treasury Secretary Morgenthau held a lengthy meeting today to discuss the U.S. silver policy and its impact on China. Recently, a telegram from Shanghai stated that Chinese Ambassador to the U.S., Dr. Shi Zhaoji, had reported to his home government that the U.S. government had agreed to change its silver purchase plan to help China. Today's meeting took place after this news was received. Hull and Morgenthau remained silent about the content of the meeting. When reporters asked Treasury Secretary Morgenthau if the U.S. would allow China to avoid a sharp increase in silver prices, he answered cautiously, saying, "This is a rumor from Shanghai. I am just doing what I have always done." Secretary of State Hull later told the Associated Press that there were no new developments in the U.S.-China silver problem negotiations, but that the two countries had recently exchanged views on the matter. However, according to powerful sources, the U.S. easing its silver purchase plan is a natural result of U.S.-China negotiations. (National News Agency, 7th)

(Hull Remains Silent on Revising Silver Purchase Program) (Washington) Secretary of State Hull told a Reuters reporter today that he knew nothing about the alleged U.S. government plan to revise its silver program to assist China. According to news from Shanghai, negotiations to amend the U.S. silver policy are currently underway. Therefore, a Reuters reporter visited Hull to inquire about this matter. (Reuters, 7th)

(No Guarantee Made to Prevent Silver Prices from Rising) (Washington) According to the Shanghai American newspaper, Chinese Ambassador to the U.S., Shi Zhaoji, has obtained assurances from the State Department that the U.S. government will try to prevent silver prices from rising again. This news has caused great surprise here. A person with special qualifications stated to Havas that the U.S. government has not made any such guarantee. (Havas, 7th)

(Reduced Coinage Tax Revenue; Purpose Not Difficult to Guess) (Washington) The silver coinage tax for the 1936 budget is only 25 million yuan, a decrease of about 75 million yuan from the estimated amount for this fiscal year. Treasury officials declined to say whether this meant that the silver purchase program would be greatly reduced, nor would they comment on whether the estimated reduction in coinage tax revenue was related to the news from Shanghai that U.S.-China negotiations are underway, asking the U.S. to pay special attention to the Chinese situation when carrying out the silver purchase program. (Reuters, 7th)

France's Attitude Towards Naval Conference: Proposes Inviting Russia and Germany to Participate

Formal Note to Washington

Japan Expresses Dissent

(Paris) The French Foreign Ministry today sent a note to Washington, with copies sent to the British and Japanese governments, stating that when negotiating a new naval treaty to replace the Washington Treaty recently abolished by Japan, naval powers such as Germany, Russia, and Spain should be invited to participate. The purpose of this French move is to determine the control of smaller navies and to eliminate the fear of any major power being left out. The full text of this note will be released when Foreign Minister Laval arrives in London. The naval issue is an important part of the Anglo-French agenda. (Reuters, 8th)

French Ambassador Visits Hirota (Tokyo) The French Ambassador to Japan, Billyard, visited Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota yesterday, expressing the French government's views on the issue of arms reduction as follows: The French government regards the Washington Treaty as a provisional treaty before 1936, with various treaties signed with reservations. However, the inferior naval power stipulated by the treaty is not satisfied, so it agrees in principle with Japan's abolition of the treaty. The international situation is different from the past. Future meetings should invite countries other than the signatory countries of the Washington Treaty, especially Germany. Foreign Minister Hirota replied that arms reduction treaties should first be concluded with major naval powers such as Britain and the United States, and then gradually extended to other countries. Even the three countries of Britain, Japan, and the United States cannot agree on their opinions in this preliminary arms reduction negotiation. Japan finds it difficult to agree to the participation of a majority of countries. (Domei, 8th)

Britain Remains Temporarily Silent (London) British officials have received a copy of the French government's note on the naval issue, stating that if this note is to be answered, it should be answered by the U.S. government. In addition, the British side believes that it is useless to re-mention the naval issue at the present time. Therefore, Britain will not give any answer to Japan in the next few weeks. However, Yamamoto, the Chief Naval Expert of the Japanese Navy, is still in London. (Havas, 7th)

British Ambassador Visits Shigemitsu

Probing Attitude Towards Naval Conference

Demands Protection for British Nationals in Eastern Provinces

(Tokyo) British Ambassador to Japan, Craigie, visited Vice Foreign Minister Shigemitsu at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs this morning at 11:00 a.m. to probe Japan's latest attitude towards the arms reduction conference and said that British nationals in the eastern provinces are being persecuted and called on the Japanese government to pay attention. (China United Press, 8th)

Enemy Air Force Difficult to Invade

Vincent Opposes Merger of Naval and Air Forces

Maintains Navy as First Line of Defense

(Washington) According to the opinion of Representative Vincent, Chairman of the House Naval Affairs Committee, in the event of war, the enemy would invade the United States by sea, but he does not believe that a strong country outside the American continent has already matured the timing to invade the United States by air. Vincent recently reported to the Federal Air Force Committee that, according to the geographical location of the United States, the enemy has no way to invade the United States except by sea. Even if they want to pass through Canada and Mexico, they must go through the sea before they can land in Canada and Mexico. Therefore, the navy will continue to be the first line of defense for the United States. Even with the recent advances in aircraft, transoceanic air raids are still an unresolved issue. Vincent supports avoiding weakening the naval air force and absolutely opposes the merger of the air force. Vincent advocates that the navy bear the full responsibility for protecting the coastline of the United States and the security of U.S. overseas territories but recognizes the need for communication between aircraft, airships, and warships. (National News Agency, 7th)

Famine in Hokkaido, Japan

Most Young Men Die in Battle in Northern Manchuria

Soybean Cakes for Food, Selling Daughters into Prostitution

(Tokyo) According to a person from Hokkaido, since the poor harvest last autumn, the entire area has fallen into a state of famine. In addition, the climate is extremely cold, and there are already feet of snow. In the past three years, affected by the period of economic recession, most of the young men, who were accustomed to the cold, were conscripted and dispatched to northern Manchuria, and many died in battle. Debts have accumulated. Now, with the double poor harvest, there is nothing to eat. Soybean cakes are imported from the northeast and have always been used as horse feed and fertilizer. Now they have become food for farmers. Some even eat tree bark, leaves, and grass roots to resist starvation. As many as 25,000 young women have been sold by their parents into prostitution. Officials are trying to cover up this fact. (China United Press, 8th)

Cuba Announces Termination of Commercial Treaty with Japan

(Tokyo) According to a report to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs by Watanabe, the Cuban Chargé d'Affaires on the 7th, the Cuban Secretary of State announced on the 5th that the provisional commercial treaty between Cuba and Japan would be terminated. As a result, this treaty will lose effect on April 5, three months after the notice of termination. Thus, Cuba and Japan have become countries without a treaty. At a time when the U.S. government is adjusting commercial relations with countries in Central and South America based on the principle of reciprocity advocated by Secretary of State Hull, the moves by Cuba and other Central and South American countries to terminate commercial relations with Japan are noteworthy. (Dentsu, 8th)

Total Funds of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Purchasing Committee

(Nanjing) According to the provisions of the exchange of notes between China and Britain, half of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity due each month is handed over to the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Purchasing Committee in London, and half is handed over to the British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees for separate safekeeping. Loans to various agencies are divided into cash loans and material purchasing loans. Except for cash loans, which are directly allocated by the Board of Trustees, for material purchasing loans, after the Board of Trustees approves the amount, it signs a contract and sends the material list to Britain for procurement. All procurement procedures, except for the material list, which must be reviewed by the Board of Trustees, are handled by the London Purchasing Committee, including bidding, contracting, signing bid agreements, selecting materials, reviewing drawings, and shipping to China. It has been learned that the total value of materials purchased by the London side for domestic agencies over the years, as of the end of last year, is approximately 2 million pounds sterling. The funds held by the Purchasing Committee, including securities, fixed deposits, and current deposits, total over 3.13 million pounds sterling. The accumulated profit and dividends are estimated at approximately 400,000 pounds sterling. (Central News Agency, 8th)

(Gold and Silver) ▲London gold price, today is one hundred and forty-two shillings, down one penny.

▲London large bars, London silver market, Chinese and Indian speculators sold out, causing the price to fall two five, but because the United States bought in the morning, the market stabilized at the close, the spot price is twenty-four pence three one two five, futures are twenty-four pence four three seven five.

▲Bombay large bars On Monday, after the announcement of the news that the U.S. budget document estimated a large reduction in silver coinage tax, the Bombay silver market opened today with considerable panic, long positions were closed, and the short side had new sales, resulting in a sharp drop in prices. The spot price opened down twelve annas to sixty-four rupees seven annas. Within half an hour, the price continued to fall to a low of sixty-three rupees ten annas, which was twenty-five annas lower than yesterday's close. However, as prices fell, buying picked up slightly, and rose three annas in the afternoon. The closing price was sixty-four rupees five annas, two annas lower than the opening price, but fourteen annas lower than yesterday's close. The market was still stable at the close.

(Exchange Rates) ▲The British and American London foreign exchange markets were quiet today, with less trading and minor fluctuations in exchange rates. The opening exchange rate between British and American currencies was four dollars, ninety cents and a half, three seven five lower than the American and British close yesterday. It rose ○ six two five at eleven o'clock, and then rose one two five at two o'clock in the afternoon. After that, there was no fluctuation. The final price was four dollars, ninety cents six eight seven five, one eight seven five higher than the opening price.

▲British-French The French franc was more active. The opening exchange rate between British and French currencies was seventy-four francs ○ three, six pounds lower. Then it rose six pounds around eleven o'clock. When they sneaked into the Bohai Institute area 40 miles northwest of Huairou, the authorities, upon receiving the report, urgently transferred the 2nd Security Brigade stationed in Miyun to prevent and block them. Xu Shiying, the brigade commander of the brigade, led the 5th Company under Mu Zisan and the 6th Company under Liu Zhenhai to head to Toudaohe, 30 miles northwest of Huairou, to block them. Seeing the government troops迎剿, the bandits lingered in Shayuli Bohai Institute and did not dare to advance. They still fled back along the original route, passing through Zhuizikou and Heishuiyu, passing through Huailai Yanqing, exiting Henglingkou and fleeing back outside the pass. The Yanqing observation army is currently dispatching troops to block them. The 2nd Security Brigade, which was dispatched to Toudaohe, has been withdrawn to its original defense yesterday because the bandits fled far away. As for the remnants of Liu Guitang's troops, they have also been severely suppressed by various armies. Some fled to the Chahar border, and some fled into the war zone, but the number is very small, and it is not difficult to eliminate them. (5th)

Shanghai Relief Association Raising Funds for Emergency Relief in Anhui Province

Anhui Investigation and Relief Office Telegraphs Request for Large Sum to Aid

First Batch Distributed to Twenty Counties Including Huaining

Anqing Correspondence: Master Hongsan and others, directors of the Anhui Province Investigation and Relief Office of the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Famine Relief in Various Provinces, after arriving in Anhui, immediately organized the Investigation and Relief Office, which was attached to the Provincial Disaster Area Fundraising and Relief Association. Previously, considering that the disaster area in Anhui Province was too large to be fully covered, they specially telegraphed the association to allocate a large sum to aid. Yesterday, they received a reply stating that the current relief funds are only 80,000 yuan, and eight or ten counties in the drought area that have recently been affected by bandits should be selected for the first batch of relief. The remaining funds will be handled after the recent supplementary allocation of relief funds. In addition, 640 new cotton-padded clothes and 160 old cotton-padded clothes will be allocated to Anhui Province. It is also reported that the office, according to the results of various investigations, has stipulated that the disaster-stricken counties in Anhui Province are divided into the most severely and next most severely affected levels, and personnel will be sent to the field in batches to investigate and provide relief. The first batch of severely affected counties that will be given priority for emergency relief are Huaining, Tongcheng, Qianshan, Taihu, Zhide, Dongliu, Qingyang, Shitai, Jingxian, Jingde, Taiping, Ningguo, Xuxi, Xiuning, Shexian, Qimen, Huoshan, Huoqiu, Lihuang, and other twenty counties, divided into ten groups. Personnel for investigation and relief will be selected soon and dispatched in different directions. The office has now convened a full meeting of the standing committee members to hold a relief work meeting, which resolved three important cases as follows: (1) When the relief funds arrive in the province, they will be stored in the Bank of China, and the withdrawal procedures will be the responsibility of one person each from the Provincial Party Headquarters, the Provincial Government, the Provincial Fundraising and Relief Association, and the Investigation and Relief Office to sign; (2) When the investigation and relief personnel arrive in each county, they will send letters to the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government, respectively, to order the party and government organs and the stationed troops to assist and protect them at any time, and also send letters to the Provincial Government to issue passports; (3) The disaster-stricken counties that have not been allocated in the first batch will be investigated and relieved when the second batch of relief funds arrives. Traitor's End: Zhao Xinbo Executed by Shooting

Invited to a Banquet by Hishikari, He Was Executed on the Spot

Shenyang Correspondence: Before Zhao Xinbo, a well-known traitor, returned from Japan after investigating constitutional government, the puppet government dismissed him from all his puppet positions last month. When Hishikari inspected the Lianpu area, Zhao happened to return. Hishikari invited Zhao to a banquet as a pretext. After Zhao arrived, he was immediately shot. Zhao's wealth from betraying the country, amounting to hundreds of thousands of gold, was also confiscated. The reasons for his death are: (1) Zhao is a talented but treacherous person. Since he can sell his motherland, what country can he not sell if given the opportunity? (2) Since the Incident, Zhao has relied on the Honjo military department as his backing, and has been very disdainful of Japanese personnel in the puppet organization. Therefore, many Japanese personnel resent him. (3) Zhao mistakenly believed that the puppet organization was a genuine country, and therefore rebuked the (Manchu) people in the puppet organs to their faces when they tried to curry favor with the Japanese. Therefore, the puppet Manchu people also resented him. (4) The puppet Supervisory Yuan wanted to investigate the Legislative Yuan under Zhao's control, but Zhao refused, which aroused dissatisfaction among the puppet organizations. As for the cause of death announced by the Japanese, they falsely accused Zhao of communicating with the interior. Currently, people in the puppet organization who relied on Zhao for support are all crestfallen and look extremely pitiful. (Northeast News Agency)

Hebei Province Strictly Prevents Liu Bandit's Return

Twelve Counties Along the Border Ravaged by Bandits

Police Teams Block and Suppress in Different Directions

Tianjin Correspondence: The remnants of Liu Guitang's troops, last month, raised the false banner of the "First Regiment Under Heaven" and roamed the borders of Hebei, once disturbing the suburbs of Pingjin. After being repelled by the Tongxian militia and stationed troops, Yu Xuezhong feared that the bandit troops would sneak into the war zone and join forces with the local bandits in Yutian County and the old troops of Shi Yousan, making it difficult to suppress them and further spreading the poisoned area. Therefore, he dispatched Zhang Yantian's troops from the newly formed Special Police Team of the War Zone stationed in Cangzhou, and transferred two companies of elite troops to pursue them. At the same time, the Baoding Xingying also dispatched two companies of the 17th Cavalry Division to advance north along the Pinghan Road to block them. The bandit troops could not stay, and because the militia of Wanping, Daxing, Tongxian, Baxian, and Pinggu five cavalry surrounded them on different routes, they changed their plan to disturb the war zone and returned to harass Huairou and Miyun. After being intercepted by the militias of these counties, they took advantage of the situation to break through and return to eastern Chahar. According to the reports received by the Hebei Provincial Government in recent days, the bandit troops seem to have entered the area between Huailai and Yanqing. Although Chahar Province has received a telegram from the Hebei Provincial Government, the blockade was not timely, and the bandits have already entered the territory. The provincial army has been dispatched to search, but no traces of the bandits have been found. The bandit troops have been roaming on the border of Hebei for more than a month, and the affected counties include Lingshou, Pingshan, Quyang, Laishui, Tangxian, Manxian, Yixian, Wanxian, Changping, Shunyi, Wanping, and Huairou, among others. Among them, Lingshou, Quyang, Tangxian, and Manxian were entered and exited by the bandit troops several times, and the number of villages looted and burned was over a hundred, which was more serious than other counties. Now, the provincial authorities are deeply afraid that the bandit troops will come again to harass. On the one hand, they are telegraphing Chahar Province for assistance in suppression, and on the other hand, they are ordering the teams of Changping, Huairou, and Miyun counties along the border to strengthen their defenses. The special police team under Zhang Yantian, which was dispatched to pursue, because the bandit troops looted horses along the way for riding, and traveled day and night, avoiding direct conflict, resulting in a large disparity between the special police's infantry and cavalry, and they were never able to catch up. The provincial order then ordered them to temporarily station in Fangshan to assist the Huaimi team in preventing and blocking.

This time, the remnants of Liu Guitang's troops were originally rebelled troops of the Chahar Army Xia Ziming. Last autumn, when Brigade Commander Xia Ziming went to Lushan for training, Liu Guitang, who was active in Tianjin, secretly sent his groom to Xia's brigade to incite rebellion. When the matter was leaked, the Chahar authorities were able to prevent it, so only two companies of cavalry mutinied, led by the bandit leader Dai battalion commander, and fled to the border of Hebei. Along the way, they recruited farmers and expanded the bandit forces as much as possible. When they harassed Pingdongbei, there were already more than 400 people. In addition to Dai battalion commander, there was also a groom of Liu Guitang and a 19-year-old teenager. The three bandit leaders were all exceptionally fierce, proficient in riding and shooting, and could open box cannons with both hands. Even in winter, they did not wear boots or shoes, but wrapped several pairs of cloth socks around their feet. Each person had several horses, so the police and groups who were harassed and on foot were often overwhelmed when they encountered them. Liu Guitang intended to have the troops mix into the war zone and establish contact with a puppet force of Shi Yousan's troops in Yutian to take a coordinated approach and prepare for recent attempts. Now that the plan has failed, the bandit troops have re-entered Chahar, still wanting to collude with the rebellion of Xia's troops stationed in Yanqing, or return to Hebei, or go far away to northern Sui to join forces with Yang Monkey Boy's bandit troops and launch an attack when the time is right. (5th)

Shandong-Hebei Border Dispute Resolved

(Public and Private Rights Equally Divided, Representatives from Two Provinces Survey and Demarcate the Border)

Jinan Correspondence: Recently, the people of Wudi in northern Shandong and Yanshan in southern Hebei have been in dispute over 150 hectares of land, and the dispute has not been resolved. The governments of the two provinces also feel that it is necessary to clarify the provincial border. Therefore, they sent representatives to Jinan to negotiate several times. Both sides presented evidence, but the problem could not be resolved. Finally, Han Fuju, chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, proposed that there was no need to argue any further. The 150 hectares of land should be divided in the middle, with each province getting 75 hectares. Public and private rights should be divided accordingly. This method was telegraphed to Yu Xuezhong, chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, for approval. Yu has replied by telegram agreeing to it, and has appointed Li Xiaoshan and Shi Mou as representatives of Hebei Province to redraw the provincial border. Han has appointed Councilor Zhao Yunxie as the representative of Shandong Province, and they will go to the junction of Wudi and Yanshan on the 7th to survey and demarcate the border, bury boundary stones, and permanently end the dispute. (6th)

Korea Hopes to Catch the Murderer in the Zhang Case Within Three Months

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Instructs Han to Catch the Murderer

Replacements Not Yet Studied

Zhang's Father, Hexuan, Has Arrived in Jinan

Jinan Correspondence: Since Zhang Weicun was assassinated on the 2nd of this month, the search for the murderer is ongoing. The provincial government previously offered a reward of 20,000 yuan for those who report inside information that leads to the solving of the case, and 50,000 yuan for those who can fully confess and solve the case. Today (6th), an additional article was added: those involved in the case who can surrender and report will be exempted from punishment and will be given a reward of 10,000 yuan. As for the suspects detained at the Jinde Association on the evening of the 2nd, most have been released. Those who are slightly more suspicious are still under investigation. Han Fuju, chairman of the provincial government, also summoned Zhang's driver and asked about the situation on the way from the Huangting Stadium to the Jinde Association on that day. It is said that nothing was found either. Today (6th), when reporters visited Han, Han said, (Since the death of Committee Member Zhang, many telegrams have been received from all parties. Today I received another telegram from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, also instructing me to strictly catch the murderer. From my observation, it seems that the murderer will not be difficult to catch. I hope the case can be solved within three months. As for whether the vacancy of the Standing Committee Member of the Provincial Party Headquarters left by Committee Member Zhang after his death will be filled in order of succession, it must be studied and then decided. Who will fill the vacancy of the Provincial Government Committee Member has not yet been studied.)

After Zhang Weicun's death, his mother and wife were both in Jinan. His father, Hexuan, was in Linyi and was telegraphed to inform him. Although Zhang's body was dressed for burial, it was only covered with the party flag without a coffin lid, waiting for his father to see him. Today (6th) at 2:00 PM, Zhang's father rushed here, lifted the flag to take a look at the place where the coffin was placed, and cried bitterly. Later, he was dissuaded by relatives and friends, and then the coffin lid was closed. Zhang Hexuan went to the provincial government to meet Han, thanking him for his concern and asking him to catch the murderer. Han deeply comforted him. Li Tianni, Cao Junfeng, Li Wenzhai, and Supervisory Committee Member Zhang Zhuxi, the directors of the funeral preparation office, convened a meeting of the office staff today (6th) to discuss funeral matters.
