The City's Important Social Construction Labor Daycare Center Opens Today

Only Daycare is Provided, No Infants are Accepted Temporarily

Mayor Wu Starts a Daycare Center for the Common People

The Penglai Road Labor Daycare Center, located near Panfang, is sponsored by the City Children's Welfare Committee. After active preparations by Director Li Ting'an, Deputy Director You Jihua, and Daycare Director Ms. Zhu Jicang, it was originally scheduled to open on the 4th. However, because the building had not yet been completed, it was decided to officially open this morning, without any ceremony. The staff had already entered the building to work, and registration and physical examinations would begin on the 10th and 11th. A reporter from the Hua Dong News Agency

Visited the center on the morning of the 8th to inquire. According to Director Zhu, because the daycare center only provides daycare, it is unable to care for newborns of one or two months. She is very sorry to those who entrust their children. Once the facilities are slightly improved, the scope will be expanded to serve the working class of this city. It is also learned that Mayor Wu, in view of the development of industry and commerce in this city, the establishment of factories, and the large number of common people, both men and women, are forced to make a living, so the safety of infants cannot be taken into account. The daycare business for the common people is one of the most important social constructions in this city at present. It has been decided to select sites in the north and south districts of the city this year to build two daycare centers for the common people, in order to seek the life safety of the working class of this city.

Firecracker Explodes and Injures People

Shen A'gen and Shen Hezhang, from Ningbo, live at No. 21 Yuhua Li, Tianbao Road, Zhabei. After becoming unemployed and struggling to make a living, they gathered their friends to make firecrackers at their residence. Because the end of the lunar year is approaching, their inventory is piled up like a mountain. In recent days, many peddlers have gone to buy goods in bulk, making the place very crowded. Yesterday afternoon at about 1:00 PM, Shen A'gen and Shen Hezhang were chatting intimately in the workshop. Hezhang, having nothing to do while sitting, lit a cigarette. Inadvertently, he threw the cigarette butt into the pile of firecrackers. After being ignited by the fire, it exploded with a bang. At the time, Shen Hezhang was directly hit by the explosion, and his face was injured by the stones. Both eyes were also affected, and blood flowed straight down. He fell to the ground in extreme pain. The doors and windows were also slightly affected. Afterwards, neighbors reported to the Linping Road Public Security Bureau, which sent police to investigate. The injured person was sent to the hospital for treatment, and Shen A'gen was taken to the bureau for questioning.

Record of the Trial of the Yu Tai-tai Kidnapping Case

Yu Tai-tai's, Who Lived in the Western A'xian Si Road French Concession at House Number Sixty, The Mother of Yu Bao-Shou, the Owner of the Yu Bao-Shan Charity Hall (26 Years Old) (Yu He Zhen-Ya, 46 Years Old), Was a Catholic. On October 21st of Last Year, At 8:00 AM, She Left Home in Her Own Car to Attend Mass at the Lu-Ban Road Catholic Church. While Traveling on the Western A'xian Si Road,

In the Middle of the Road Opposite Numbers 29 and 31 Near the Third High Court, Several Kidnappers Who Had Been Lying in Ambush There Suddenly Rushed Up, Kidnapped Her, and Fled. The Victim Was Hidden Away and a Letter Sent to the Family Demanding a Huge Sum of Money for Her Release. On November 19th, the Kidnappers Contacted the Family in the San Xin Hotel Outside the Su Zhou Lu Men Gate to Negotiate the Ransom. The French Police, Having Received a Report From the Family, Sent Detectives Disguised as Family Representatives With Two Bottles of Hua Diao Wine and Five Tins of Red Tin Pack Cigarettes to Serve as a Secret Code, as Agreed With the Kidnappers. Upon Arrival in Suzhou, the Kidnappers, Li Chun-Xiao From Shao-Xing, and Wang Fu-Kang From Hu Zhou, Were Arrested at the Train Station. They Were Sent to the Public Security Bureau in Charge. They Revealed That the Victim Was Hidden in the Loft of Number 368 Yu-Lin Road in the Public Concession. Immediately, a Long-Distance Call Was Made to the French Police, Who Sent Chinese and Foreign Detectives to Work With the Yu-Lin Road Police to Go to the Address, Rescue the Victim, and Arrest the Kidnappers Guarding Her, Zhang Hui-Zhi From Shao-Xing, Tao Shui-Gen, Lin De, and a Woman, Zhou Ju-Qin, Four People in All. During the Arrest, Both Tao and Lin Fired Their Guns in Resistance and Were Injured. At the Same Time, Patrolman Zhang Chun-Sheng, Number 47, Was Shot in the Left Knee While Trying to Subdue Them. All the Injured Were Sent by Car to the Guang Ci Hospital. That Night, the Detectives Went to Suzhou and Transferred the Two Kidnappers, Li and Wang, to Shanghai. The Next Day, They Were Taken to the Second Special Court for Questioning and Detention for Investigation. Later, the Injured Kidnapper, Tao Shui-Gen, Died on the 28th of the Same Month After Medical Treatment Proved Ineffective. The Court Was Notified and an Autopsy Was Performed, After Which the Body Was Placed in a Coffin by a Charitable Organization. Because the Victim Was Sick and Frightened and the Injured Lin Could Not Be Investigated, the Police Repeatedly Asked the Court to Reschedule the Hearing. All These Details Have Been Reported in Previous Newspapers. It Is Now Learned That Lin Has Recovered From His Injuries. The Police Have Brought Him Back for a Thorough Investigation, Which Has Now Concluded. Yesterday, Judge Xiong Hui-Ping of the Second Special Court, Together With Court Clerk Tao Zong-Kan, Re-Examined the Case in Courtroom One of the Criminal Division. Yu Tai-Tai, Because She Was Shocked, Became Ill, and Although She Has Recovered and Been Discharged From the Hospital, Her Mental State Has Not Yet Recovered and She Has Left Shanghai to Recuperate in Another City. Therefore, She Was Not Present in Court. First, the Police Lawyer Gu Shou-Xi Gave a Detailed Account of the Police Investigation, Prosecuting Li, Wang, Zhang, and Zhou Under Article One, Section One of the Law for the Punishment of Bandits. The Crime of Murder Under the Law for the Punishment of Bandits, Article One, Section One, and Article 282 of the Criminal Law is Used to Charge Lin De. The Court Asked for Further Information, Ordered Each Prisoner to Be Brought Down for Separate Interrogation. First, Wang Fu-Kang Testified That the Kidnapping Was Initiated by Yu Yong-Xiang From Outside. They Discussed It at the Asian Hotel and That Wang Bao-Rui (That is, The One Who Wrote the Letter to the Family Demanding the Ransom, Using the Name of Hong Jun Commander-In-Chief Wang Bao-Rui) And the Driver Li A-Mao And I Were at the Scene Discussing the Kidnapping, Zhang Fu-Gen, Yu Yong-Xiang, Lin De, Tao Shui-Gen, The Driver Li A-Mao And I Went Together to the House Where the Victim Was Being Held, Which Was Rented By Yu Yong-Xiang. Tao Shui-Gen, Lin De, Zhang Hui-Zhi, Etc. Were Guarding the Victim. Zhang Hui-Zhi Is a Carpenter and Was Called There By Tao Shui-Gen. Zhou Ju-Qin Was Also Called There By Tao Shui-Gen to Be a Cook. Yu Yong-Xiang And I Went to Suzhou Together to Negotiate the Ransom. Li Chun-Xiao Met Him in Suzhou and Did Not Participate in the Kidnapping. I Don't Know That the Police Fired a Gun to Resist Arrest When They Went to Arrest Him. Li Chun-Xiao Testified That He Knew Wang Fu-Kang From Xiao-Shan in the Past. I Don't Know About the Kidnapping. This Time, I Met Wang Fu-Kang on Shi Lu in Suzhou. I Asked Him Where He Was Going. He Said He Was Going to Shanghai. Because We Are Old Friends, I Sent Him to the Train Station. When the Train Came, He Didn't Get on. I Asked Him Why He Didn't Get on, and He Said He Had to Wait a While. Then He Was Arrested By the Detectives. Lin De Testified That I Didn't Go When the Kidnapping Happened. Zhang Fu-Gen Called Me to Guard the Victim. When the Detectives Came to Arrest Me, I Fired a Gun. [The Judge] Asked, The Bullet That Injured Patrolman Number 47 Has Been Proven by the Police to Have Been Fired From the Gun You Were Holding. [Lin De] Answered, I Only Fired One Shot. The Person Immediately Fell Down and I Could Not Fire a Second Shot. Zhang Hui-Zhi Testified That Yu Fu-Gen Called Me to Be a Carpenter in the Loft of Number 368 Yu-Lin Road. Zhou Ju-Qin Was Called There By Tao Shui-Gen. I Used to Work in a Cotton Mill in Yang-Shu-Pu. After Questioning to This Point, Because It Was Already Late, the Court Ordered the Trial to Be Continued in a Special Court on the Afternoon of the 10th (That is, Tomorrow). The Accused Were Still Detained and the Court Adjourned.

Ou Jialu Robbers Confess to Committing the Crime

Fifty Yuan of Stolen Money Was Distributed

Peng Zhenxuan, a Chinese detective from the Yulin Road Police Station, learned that Zhang Rui-xi, a Ningbo native from No. 7 Oujia Road, had conspired with others to rob Wang Bingjun of 1,630 yuan in silver at San Yi Li, Weituoma Road, at 7:15 PM on May 15th of last year. He reported this to the police chief, and, together with a Western detective, secretly went to the address at about 1:00 AM and arrested him. He was taken to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, he was taken to the Criminal Court 3 of the First Special Court. The Council of Public Works lawyer Li Zhishan recounted the previous events and stated that the defendant had confessed that his accomplice, Shi Caifu, was hiding at No. 254 Chang'an Road, Zhabei, and had also been arrested. They had reported this to the Public Security Bureau in charge and requested a postponement of the case. When questioned, the defendant confessed that the gun presented in the case was stored by the fugitive Lao Tou Ni Fukun because it was inconvenient for him to keep it at home as he was selling red pills. Regarding the robbery on Weituoma Road, he said that Xiao Biao was the leader and there were seven or eight people in total. Afterwards, I received 50 yuan, which is the truth. Judge Feng Shide instructed that he should remain in custody and the case should be verified further.

He sent detectives Liu Junxi, detectives Lang Chengpei, and patrolmen Wang Yifei and Wang Rulin to Jiujiudi, where they arrested the bandit Sun A'tu. The detectives went to the address and successively arrested five accomplices, Chen A'si, Dong A'mao, Huang Jicheng, Zhang Xiaomao, and Zhang Linhua. A pistol and 15 bullets were found on Chen A'si. It was said that Wang Ren supplied the gun and bullets. The detectives then went to No. 13 Cheng Zhi Li, Yangjia Lane, Xinbeimen, to arrest Wang and take him back to the Lao Zha Police Station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were taken to the Criminal Court 1 of the First Special Court. Old America's Most Stylish Women's Shoe Store Grand Competition

Old America's Most Stylish has always been a leading brand in women's shoes. Its original location was at the corner of Sanma Road and Guangxi Road. Last year, due to the expiration of the lease, it built a new, artistically designed store and moved to the opposite side of the small garden on Guangxi Road. This January marks the 15th anniversary of the store's opening. The store has specially made various stylish flannel warm shoes and is holding a grand competition for one month. During this period, customers will not only receive a 20% discount on all sizes but will also have a public lottery every night with excellent prizes. It is said that the method is that all invoices issued are numbered, and if the last digit of a customer's invoice number matches the drawn number (a total of ten numbers from 1 to 10), they will receive any product of the same value as the original invoice purchase, still be treated as a purchase, and then have another invoice issued to participate in another lottery, so that it is continuous. The excellence of the products, the novelty of the styles, the low prices, and the speed of ordering are secondary.

Organization of the Destitute Children's Work-Study Group

There are many poor children in Shanghai who are out of school and unemployed, lacking both the ability to make a living and the opportunity to study. This is not a blessing for society. Recently, several colleagues in the field of social education, in view of this, have specially organized a Destitute Children's Work-Study Group. During the day, they will teach commercial knowledge and carry goods for sale, using the surplus profits to maintain their lives. In the evening, they will provide two hours of classes, waiving tuition fees, so that both education and living can be solved, realizing the urgent needs of society. Those who are interested can obtain the articles of association and registration forms from the Construction Bookstore on Bai'er Road, west of Nanyang Bridge, in this city.

New and Old Works by Chen Zhuzun

Mr. Chen Zhuzun, a professor at Jiaotong University, has written "Supplement to Mozi's Informal Talks," which is about six to seven hundred thousand words long. It collects about hundreds of books on Mozi from Sun Zhongrong onwards, in order to supplement Sun's book. Modern scholars such as Chen Shiyi and Tang Weizhi all believe that it is sufficient to compile a great compendium of Mohist studies. The book was previously submitted to the Commercial Press, and the typesetting and proofreading had been completed, but it had not yet been bound. During the January 28th Incident, it perished along with the national crisis. Scholars lamented it. Now, it is said that Mr. Chen has been engaged in restoring this book for three years, in addition to teaching, and has added new acquisitions in recent times. It is now almost complete and will be carefully proofread during the winter vacation and re-submitted to the Commercial Press for publication. After this book is completed, it is said that Mr. Chen intends to write a "Collected Annotations on Guanzi" in the style of Wang Xianqian's "Collected Annotations on Xunzi," as there is no good edition of the book "Guanzi." He has now collected a wealth of works on Guanzi.

The Deadline for Pre-ordering the Western-Style Four Series Essential Book is at the End of the Month

The Four Series Essential Book printed by the Zhonghua Book Company in the Ju Zhen Imitation Song Edition has long been appreciated by the literary world. Last spring, the pre-sale of the five-open edition was oversubscribed. The fact that our country's ancient books can be widely circulated and popularized in all walks of life, and the deep love for our inherent culture, are all worthy of praise. Now, in response to the requests of various schools and libraries, the Company has re-printed the Western-style Four Series Essential Book, using a four-leaf-in-one page photocopy of the original printed five-open edition, printed on "Ci Dao Lin" paper, and rubber-stamped with security marks. The entire book contains 351 titles, totaling more than 11,300 volumes. The pre-order price is only two and a half cents per volume, which is unprecedentedly low. Moreover, for schools with insufficient funds and aspiring scholars, a payment plan in installments has been specially formulated. By saving more than ten yuan a month, one can purchase a copy in two or three years. If it is used as a commemorative gift or purchased by families to pass on to their children, the meaning is even more profound. Therefore, there are many orders from various places. The price is now set low, and the collection is easy, and the font size is moderate. There are three types of binding: A, B, and C. The original price of the A-type cloth-covered gold-lettered edition is 720 yuan, but the pre-order price is only 360 yuan. The B-type cloth-covered printed-lettered edition is 640 yuan, and the pre-order price is 320 yuan. The C-type paper-covered and bound edition is 560 yuan, and the pre-order price is 280 yuan. The deadline is the end of this month. Those who wish to pre-order, please do so as soon as possible. Sample copies of the book can be obtained from the Company.

Li Yingbiao's Book (Coke) Published

Dr. Li Yingbiao, an expert in steel engineering who studied in Belgium and is currently the Chief of General Affairs of the Nanjing Municipal Health Office, has recently published a book titled (Coke), which contains his years of learning and experience. The content is divided into: (1) The Origin of Coke Production, (2) The Production of Coke, (3) A Brief Diagram of the Extraction of By-products and Utilization of Residual Heat from Coke Production, (4) The Xuanmei Solvay Oven, (5) Coke Ovens for Extracting By-products and Utilizing Waste Steam, (6) A General Discussion of Ordinary Coke Ovens, (7) The Theory of Compression. The text is more than 10,000 words long, with outstanding insights and detailed elaboration. The cover is inscribed by Wang Jingqi, former Chinese Envoy to Belgium, and it is printed by the Jinling Printing House in Huangnigang, Nanjing. The price is fixed at five dimes per copy. The general agent in this city is the Dagong Bao Agency Department at No. 322 Jiujiang Road. The following is an excerpt from its introduction: In the past hundred years, our country has been in hardship and distress, forced into economic oppression by the great powers, with backward industries and extreme poverty. However, in terms of national defense construction, even the most skilled woman would find it difficult to cope. Even military supplies rely on the agricultural sector facing an empty granary. Therefore, the key to addressing the root cause of poverty and weakness is to seek ways to become rich and strong. Mr. Wu Zhihui once encouraged our people with the eight characters (Everyone is responsible for industrial planning), as the common goal to pursue in the future. I deeply admire his incisive words. However, the implementation of industrial planning requires steel everywhere, and steel is made from cast iron. The smelting of cast iron cannot be accomplished without the supply of a large amount of coke. Therefore, the production of coke is one of the most important things in revitalizing industry, which is clearly evident. With our country's rich resources, considering the current market value of coke, setting up factories to manufacture it is already profitable just from pure charcoal. Moreover, there are by-products such as ammonia, which can be used to make fertilizers for farmland; black oil, which is necessary for building roads; and gas, which can be used for fuel engines, enough to plug the loopholes and recover rights and interests, which would be of great benefit to people's livelihood and the national economy. Now, I will extract the experience I have gained and describe in detail the construction of coke ovens, the production of coke, the extraction of by-products, and the selection of coke ovens, as well as the factory construction plan, etc., and add a general discussion. This is a rough draft, and there will be many errors. If you can point them out, I would be very grateful.

(City Voices) ▲ Domestic Calcium Carbonate Sells Well Calcium carbonate is an important raw material in rubber products, and it used to be imported from Japan, which had a significant impact on the rubber industry. In recent years, domestic calcium carbonate has been temporarily promoted. Chen Xiaoping, the manager of the Xinyue Chemical Factory in this city, has been enthusiastically researching and manufacturing calcium carbonate, which is of high purity and lower price than Japanese products, so it is very popular among factories. Although Japanese products are being sold at low prices, the factory is also enduring sacrifices, which has greatly hit the sales of Japanese products, adding a lot of glory to the domestic products industry. Recently, due to the cold and rainy weather, it has been difficult to ship the goods, so the factory has specially built a drying room to replace sun drying. Although the cost has increased, the selling price is still cheaper than Japanese products, it is said.

(Publishing World) ▲ Detailed Explanation of Trigonometry is About to be Published The book "Trigonometry" by Mr. Seuses III of the United States is valued for its precise content, and many bookstores have translated the original book into Chinese for use as a textbook, such as "Trigonometry" by Zhonghua, "Saisiusi" by Nanjing, and "Plane Geometry" by Beiping Culture. Now, Zhang Zhaoyun, a mathematics teacher at Jingye Middle School, in order to facilitate teachers' reference and students' self-study, has made a detailed explanation of all 1,500 questions in the exercises. The content and organization are generally calculated by section, so that each book can be used universally. The solution methods strive for novelty and clarity, with more than 1,000 illustrations. It is currently being bound and is scheduled to be released in early January. Sample copies are available for request from the Xueyi Society of Shanghai Jingye Middle School (Pai'ai).

Letter

To the esteemed Editor, Since the beginning of winter, it is common to see reports in newspapers of people dying from coal poisoning due to using coal briquettes to heat their homes. The reports are incessant. It has been found that coal poisoning can cause people to faint and lose their breath, which is a state of suspended animation, not true death. If sauerkraut soup or sauerkraut is used to resuscitate the person who has lost their breath, no matter how deep the poisoning, they can be awakened immediately. This is a method that has been used in Beijing for hundreds of years and is extremely effective. Because there are such unfortunate events happening in this city every day, and no one is being saved, I really cannot remain silent. I am specially writing to your newspaper to promote this widely and create happiness for the people. If there is no sauerkraut soup, salty vegetable brine can also be used for resuscitation, which can also be effective, but not as effective as sauerkraut soup. This is to the esteemed Editor of the Shen Bao, Qu Mei kowtows, January 6th.

To the esteemed Editor, Regarding the news item (Collection of Fisheries Construction Fee Fails; Dai Yongdian Accused of Ignoring Funds) published in the news column of your newspaper on the 6th of this month, I was shocked to read it. The case of Jin Gengyao suing Yong Tang is because Yong Tang and Jin are both shareholders of the Hangzhou Wanchun Fish Firm. This lawsuit is entirely a dispute between partners in a joint venture. Yong Tang is currently in the midst of a criminal counterclaim. It is purely a private matter and has nothing to do with the Fisheries Construction Fee Collection Office. However, the words in your newspaper's report that involve the Fisheries Construction Fee Collection Office are prone to misleading people. It is thought that the information was inaccurate. Therefore, I am specially writing to request that you make a factual correction to avoid misrepresentation. This is my earnest plea. With best regards, Dai Yongtang respectfully, January 8th, 24th year.

Spring and Autumn

Little West Heaven

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 7: Hearing Words, She Covers Her Tears and Sells Herself to Endure Bitterness; Carefully Observing, She Seeks to Join the East and Earnestly Hopes for Kindness

Cheng Zhi looked at Sister Hu and said, "Just look at her state, she certainly won't mind this matter, so there's no need to worry about that. It's just that when he and Xiao Ji wanted that money, Xiao Ji denied it with a blank face, saying it was just a joke. They're not..." He paused, and then said, "I can't bear to say these words. But I thought this girl was here to get married, and whether it succeeds or not is a matter for the two families, so why should the matchmaker pay out of their own pocket? If they want a dollar for every trip, that's easy, the teahouse servants can think of other ways with him. But Xiao Ji can't speak as tactfully as I do. This girl is the same age as us, and instead of getting money, she's subjected to such an insult. Isn't that pitiful? To be honest, what kind of marriage is this? It's just selling her body to get a bowl of rice for three generations. When a person has nothing else to sell, and they have to sell their own body, that's always a heartbreaking thing. If there's good news, it means her body has found a buyer..." Suddenly, there were several very low sobs nearby. It turned out that Miss Yueying, overcome with sadness, was shedding tears like a pouring rain. She didn't dare to use the clothes she was wearing to wipe her tears, because those clothes were borrowed. She had to pull out the sleeve of the clothes she was wearing underneath to wipe away the tears. Cheng Zhi was also speaking with great enthusiasm, and he had forgotten whether the girl sitting in front of him could bear what he was saying. Now that Yueying was crying, he realized that he had spoken too freely, so he immediately cleared his throat and smiled, "That was my mistake, Miss, please don't take it to heart. Otherwise, when Sister Hu and Xiao Ji were arguing, I wouldn't have let you into the room." (107)

Yuan Xiaoyou's Extreme Advocacy for Concubinage

— Wang Yun

Those who take concubines must be crying out, "Injustice! It's unjust!" Concubines have no legal status. The head of the family spends a lot of money on the bride price and pays alimony, but still cannot claim her as his own. Recently, the Supreme Court's Unified Law Interpretation Committee interpreted that if a concubine commits adultery, the head of the family has no right to sue. Then all the heads of families who take concubines should all cry out in unison, "Injustice! It's unjust!" As the old saying goes, "(Stolen gongs and drums cannot be played loudly)." Clearly, it's your own concubine, but she becomes like stolen gongs and drums, and even if she has an affair with someone else, you can't speak out. Doesn't this mean willingly wearing a green hat? But don't worry, heads of families who take concubines. I will record the memorial submitted by Yuan Xiaoyou, who praised concubinage during the Tuoba Wei Dynasty in the Northern History, giving the general idea. I think that when the heads of families who take concubines see it, they will definitely laugh through their tears.

(In ancient times, the feudal lords married nine women, and the scholars had one wife and one concubine. The Jin decree stated that the princes could marry eight concubines, and the marquises could marry six concubines. The official decree stated that the first and second ranks had four concubines, the third and fourth ranks had three concubines, the fifth and sixth ranks had two concubines, and the seventh and eighth ranks had one concubine. Therefore, yin teachings were cultivated, and the succession was extensive. Extensive succession is filial piety. Cultivating yin teachings is propriety. [Omission] Nowadays, people generally have no standards! When parents marry off their daughters, they teach them jealousy. Aunts and sisters greet each other and advise each other to be jealous, in order to control the husband as a woman's virtue, and to be able to be jealous as a woman's skill. If the husband's heart of jealousy arises, then the propriety between wife and concubine will be abandoned, and the signs of adultery will increase. This is what I hate and regret. I request that the princes and dukes be the first rank, marrying eight concubines, so as to prepare for the affairs of the nine women. The second rank should prepare seven, the third and fourth ranks should prepare five, and the fifth and sixth ranks should have two wives and two concubines... Princes, marquises, generals, ministers, meritorious officials, descendants of sons and daughters, should fill the court, and the succession should be endless. This is my ambition.) If Yuan Xiaoyou's proposal were passed in today's Legislative Yuan, those who have taken concubines could all rejoice and shout several times "(Long live concubinage)!" Unfortunately, this is just a historical article!

Tidbits

— (Xia Cenjuan)

Before the three brothers married, they loved each other like hands and feet. But after each of them got married and started a family, they often quarreled and scolded each other all day long. The reason for this is that they all listened to what their wives said in bed. As a result, they divided the family property and went to court, and loving brothers became enemies. Liu Xuande in the Romance of the Three Kingdoms said, "A wife is like clothes, and brothers are like hands and feet. Clothes can be mended if they are torn, but hands and feet cannot be reattached if they are broken." This statement is not very accurate. You must know that in modern times, brothers are seen as cheap assets, while wives are seen as precious boats!

In the Waiting Room

— Wu Liao'an

The market is extremely bleak and depressed, but the waiting room in the court is strangely bustling!

Ding-ling! Ding-ling! As soon as the bell for office hours rang, the waiting room was already crowded with men, women, old people, and young people, all waiting to be judged by the law.

On the face of each of these people, there was a kind of worried, fearful, and silent expression, each different, as well as the ferocious faces and arrogant attitudes of the creditors. If we were to capture all of this in a camera, what a profound expression of the faces it would be!

A Western-dressed man, covered in filth, with a snow-white hard collar that had almost turned black. His hair was long like an artist's, and his face was haggard and pale, with no smile at all. He sat silently in the left corner of the waiting room. On the seat opposite him, a frivolous and fashionable modern woman often showed a self-satisfied state to him and sometimes even sneered at him. It turned out that the two of them were the main characters in a divorce case! Some of the people waiting were gossiping, taking them as conversation material, whispering and guessing.

XXX, XXX, when the names of the parties were shouted loudly by a stern-looking bailiff to begin the hearing, it immediately broke through the clamor in the waiting room, and it became so quiet that even the sound of breathing could be heard. The blood of each of the waiting defendants would suddenly become tense, fearing to hear their own name. But how could that be possible? Finally, they were summoned to be tried one by one!

Ding-ling! Ding-ling! The bell for the end of office hours was ringing! The sound of people in the waiting room changed from bustling to silent, as silent as the depressed market.

The Security of Imperialism

Remembering the Qiusheng Building

— Zhengdong

Everyone knows Ouyang Xiu's "Ode to the Sound of Autumn"; this summer, while traveling in Yu, I unintentionally discovered the Qiusheng Building, so I recorded it as follows.

The Qiusheng Building is located in Huaxian, northern Yu, about eighteen li from Daokou. There is a county road that can be accessed, so transportation is still considered convenient. Enter the south gate and travel a few hundred paces to reach the Ouyang Academy; it is now the County First Primary School. There is an ancient stele in front of the gate, engraved with the words "The Place Where Ouyang Wenzhong Gong of the Song Dynasty Studied," which was written by the local county magistrate. Inside, there is a room; on the wall is embedded a blue stone, engraved with the full text of "Ode to the Sound of Autumn." Further in is the Qiusheng Building; the plaque in front of the building is still new. When asked, it was said that it was recently re-inscribed because the previous one was destroyed in the rebellion of 1927. The building has a stone base, so it is quite sturdy. Facing south, there are three wooden windows. Inside, the room is very empty, the stairs have been destroyed, and above is the library; according to legend, there were more than two thousand books before, but they were all destroyed in the war of 1927. To this day, not a single scrap remains. The roof is rectangular in shape and not very wide. It is currently the principal's office, but during the summer vacation, all items have been moved out. Outside, the roof is covered with weeds, the scene is desolate. Behind it are several houses, all used as classrooms. The courtyard has been occupied by soldiers for a long time, and everything has been destroyed. Although it has been repaired, the doors and windows are still messy and uneven, and there is nothing worth recording. Therefore, I will omit it.

In the southwest of the courtyard, there is an ancient temple from the Sui Dynasty, which was later destroyed in the White Lotus Rebellion of the Qing Dynasty; now, only an ancient pagoda remains, its top bald, and the pagoda body is tilted and about to collapse. The authorities ignore the historical sites, causing the buildings of previous generations to be destroyed day by day. It is truly lamentable!

御香縹緲錄

— Translated from the original by Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou

But don't underestimate this simple palace! It really occupies a very important position in the history of the Manchus! The Empress Dowager also regarded it as an antique with great commemorative value. As soon as we walked in, she immediately pointed east and west, explaining all the arrangements and decorations to us piece by piece, and she spoke very fluently and thoughtfully, as if she had been here several times before; in fact, she was visiting for the first time, just like us! It is a pity that there was no one who was truly familiar with the history of our clan at this time, because if there were, it would not be difficult to immediately judge the truth of the Empress Dowager's words. However, although I cannot guarantee whether the story about the hunting ground is true, her knowledge is indeed frighteningly broad at times, and many of them are true facts, which cannot be denied! She often prides herself on her extensive knowledge and strong memory. Whenever she has something more unusual to tell us, she often speaks with extraordinary eloquence, for fear of failing to move us. This attitude is actually a manifestation of a woman's vanity, but she herself doesn't realize it!

Inside this palace, large story paintings are painted on every wall with various colors of oil paint. Although their colors have become very dull due to the passage of time, and the brushwork of the paintings is also very crude, the outlines can still be considered clear, and the postures and expressions of the people in the paintings can still express seventy or eighty percent of their original intent. These murals are in all three rooms. The Empress Dowager led us along, explaining these paintings to us, which turned out to be all hunting portraits of past Manchu leaders. (217)

Miscellaneous talk

Mr. Wu Zhihui's Clean Argument

— Ye Xianyun

Mr. Wu Zhihui, a supervisory committee member, gave a speech at our Zhenjiang Provincial Medical and Political College the other day. His remarks about the Japanese were quite interesting, and I will describe them as follows: "We are suffering a great loss from the Japanese now. But they do have several advantages; for example, they love to use domestic products. But this is not their primary advantage. Their greatest advantage lies in the word 'cleanliness'. The meaning of the word 'cleanliness' includes cleanliness and neatness. They are clean at all times and in all places. The cleanliness of houses goes without saying, and even the villages are very clean. I can use a joke to describe it: take their latrines as an example; the wooden boards on the pit in their latrines are so clean that you can actually squat down and play Go on them. Their walls are made of mud, and some are still in the style of our ancient China, which is very economical, and the layout is also very neat and clear. For example, when building a Western-style house, everything conforms to the Western style, but even the smallest nail is entirely their own domestic product, so Japan is an unusual nation. Their houses have mud walls below and wooden boards above, which is very much in line with the principle of simplicity and economy. For example, if you go to see them, take off your shoes and enter, it is the living room. After a while, you eat a meal, and you eat here. When it gets dark, you turn over the cabinet next to you and you can sleep. Although this is only one room, it has several uses for people, and it is so clean inside that there is nothing messy, because they get rid of everything that is useless. Japanese servants on ships throw wine bottles, cookie tins, and other miscellaneous items straight into the sea. But our Cantonese servants hide everything. So the Japanese are really poor, which corresponds to our old saying, 'a house with bare walls'. On the other hand, in our country's villages, people are always reluctant to throw away broken stools with three legs. For example, some shops on the streets of Shanghai, such as ham shops, still hang up the leftover leg and foot, and the old worn mat of the wasp's nest, or place them there securely.

On the one hand, they throw away a lot of junk, but on the other hand, their manufacturing capabilities are also surprisingly successful, and new and good things are often produced, and their competitiveness is also very fierce. For example, to buy a sheet on the British cotton market costs seven and a half shillings, but to get it from Japan only costs two and a half shillings. Everyone knows that German goods are the most exquisite items in the world. Japan desperately imitates them, and the quality is not far off, but the price is several times cheaper. The water conservancy in the Netherlands is very developed, so they need a lot of water pipes. Originally, they bought them from Belgium. From Belgium to the Netherlands is about the same as from Zhenjiang to Nanjing, which is very close. But Japan shipped them from a very long distance, and the price was cheaper, so the Netherlands adopted Japanese water pipes. Think about it, isn't it scary? Isn't it fierce? Furthermore, Shanghai foreigners like to hire Japanese or Belgian maids. People generally think that foreign women are very extravagant, but this is a big mistake. I have lived in Belgium. Middle-class families there do not have the custom of hiring servants. The landlady of the house where I lived, her husband was an engineer in an electrical factory and earned eight pounds a week, but she did everything herself. She even shined our leather shoes for us. She got up early in the morning, did other people's things first, and then did her own hair, cooked, read the newspaper, and summarized current events for us to listen to. After we finished eating and went out, she cleaned our room, cleaned the carpet, wiped the oilcloth, and wiped the doorway. She also had to wipe the streets in front of the door. They first washed them thoroughly with a lot of water, then scrubbed them with a brush, and finally wiped them with a towel, but the towel that had been wiped was not very dirty. British women are also diligent, but they are not as good as Belgian women. Therefore, if our country wants to survive, it must follow the example of the Japanese and stand on cleanliness."

Sports News

Forty-One Countries Sign Up for Next Year's Berlin World Games

Hitler Appointed Honorary President

Tickets for the Games Have Already Gone on Sale

(Berlin Correspondence) The 11th World Olympic Games will be held in Berlin starting on August 1st next year. The German side is sparing no effort in its preparations. German leader Hitler has agreed to serve as the honorary president of the Games. Tickets for next year's Games went on sale in Berlin on January 1st of this year. Switzerland has also decided on the number of athletes it will send. Interest in the upcoming Games is very high.

▲Hitler Appointed Honorary President

Due to the past practices of previous Games, and in order to respect the Olympic Games, which is an important means of promoting peace and cooperation among nations, the head of state of the host country is always the honorary president of that Games. At the 1908 Games in London, King Edward VII of England was the honorary president of the Games. At the 1912 Games in Stockholm, King Gustav V of Sweden was the honorary president. At the 1920 Games in Antwerp, King Albert of Belgium was the honorary president. At the 1924 Games in Paris, French President Doumergue was the honorary president. At the 1928 Games in Los Angeles, US President Hoover was the honorary president. In the spring of 1933, the late German President Hindenburg also accepted the honorary presidency of the 1936 Games, but unfortunately, he passed away due to illness. Now, leader Hitler, due to President Hindenburg, has accepted the position of inheritance, and has sent a letter to the chairman of the organizing committee, Dr. Li Huade, expressing his enthusiasm for care.

▲Welcome to All Countries to Participate in Football

On November 17, 1934, the Executive Committee of the International Football Association resolved to authorize the football associations of its affiliated countries to participate in the Berlin Football Championship. This resolution has confirmed that football will be one of the championship events of the 1936 Berlin Olympic Games. The German Football Association was very pleased to hear this, and Chairman Li Mann sent a letter to the football associations of all countries affiliated with the International Football Association, asking them to accept this resolution and accept the invitation of the German Olympic Committee. In order to enhance the relationship between the football associations of various countries and fulfill the friendship of the host, the German Football Association stated that it would lead 15,000 German football associations to welcome the football teams of various countries to Germany to participate.

▲Torch Relay Enthusiastically Participating

The Olympic committees of Greece, Yugoslavia, Austria, Czechoslovakia, Bulgaria, and Hungary have all agreed to participate in the Olympic torch relay run before the opening of the 1936 Berlin Games. The route and allocation of athletes will be decided or changed at the national conferences in March.

▲Tickets for the Games Have Already Gone on Sale

After the newspapers announced in November that tickets for the Games would go on sale in advance starting on January 1, 1935, the number of reservations reached more than one hundred within a week. The value of cash and checks amounted to more than a thousand pounds. To this day, the numbers are even more impressive. However, these pre-sold tickets are only limited to competitions held in the large stadium, such as the opening and closing ceremonies of the Games, track and field events, football and outdoor handball semi-finals and finals, and other performances. Swimming, boxing, fencing, and rowing competitions held outside the stadium are not pre-sold. Season tickets for each sport of the Games will not be available until July 1, 1935. Tickets for the large stadium are divided into three classes: Class A is 100 marks, Class B is 60 marks, and Class C is 40 marks. Group discounts are also available.

▲Two More Countries Accept Invitations Recently, two more countries, the Irish Free State and Monaco, have approached the Games and accepted invitations to participate. At present, a total of 41 countries have signed up to participate. The only country that declined to participate was Judea. According to the reply from Gil Kisch, chairman of the Judean Olympic Committee, the Judean Olympic Committee was established not long ago and is still in its infancy and training period, so it is very difficult to participate in 1936. He hopes to see everyone in the future.

▲Sweden Sends 2,000 People for Calisthenics

As a result of recent discussions between the Swedish Gymnastics Association and the German Organizing Committee, it was decided that two teams of men and women would be sent to Berlin to perform Swedish-style freehand exercises and calisthenics. If accommodation is not a problem, each team will have 1,000 people. The performance will be around the afternoon of August 8, 1936. The number of athletes sent by one country to the Olympic Games will be a new era. This great plan can only be admired.

▲Number of Swiss and Finnish Athletes

The number of athletes that Switzerland and Finland will send in the future has been determined as follows:

▲Switzerland

Shooting 25 people, cycling 14 people, wrestling 7 people, swimming 12 people, gymnastics 15 people, ice skating 6 people, hockey 15 people, fencing 12 people, freestyle cycling 12 people, rowing 12 people, boxing 8 people, ice hockey 12 people, track and field 21 people, weightlifting 15 people, rowing 26 people, basketball 7 people, plus equestrian and coaches 69 people, representatives 9 people, totaling 219 people.

▲Finland

Track and field 40 people, skating 16 people, wrestling 14 people, gymnastics 13 people, basketball 13 people, ice hockey 11 people, swimming 10 people, ice jumping 9 people, small boat 9 people, boxing 8 people, freestyle cycling 6 people, shooting 4 people, totaling 153 people.

▲Peru

Peru has signed up to participate in the Games. This is Peru's first time participating in the Olympic Games. The 400th anniversary of Lima, the capital of Peru, will be held in 1935, and a grand sports meet will be held at that time. Athletes will be selected at that time.

▲Latvia

Latvia has decided to participate in various winter competitions, track and field, wrestling, boxing, weightlifting, shooting, freestyle cycling, and basketball. All aspects of the work are actively being prepared.

Education News

Both Mr. Jiang and Mr. Liu, Representatives Attending the East Asia Higher Education Conference, Have Returned to Shanghai

▲Mr. Jiang Menglin Went to Beijing Last Night to Report to the Ministry of Education

▲Deeply Moved by Visiting Many Rural Areas in the Philippines

▲Filipinos Have No Problem with Livelihood and Education is Also Universal

Mr. Jiang Menglin and Mr. Liu Zhanen, representatives of our country to the East Asia Higher Education Conference in the Philippines, returned to Shanghai at 2:00 pm the day before yesterday on the Jesson. (The rumor that Mr. Liu was delayed in returning is not true.) Mr. Jiang took the night train to Beijing last night to report on the situation to the Ministry of Education and will return to Pingjin immediately. Our Shanghai reporter met with Mr. Jiang at the New Asia Hotel yesterday and discussed the experience in the Philippines in detail. The details are recorded as follows:

▲Conference Experience Mr. Jiang First Talked About This Conference Was Proactively Convened by the Philippines, Purely for the Exchange of Opinions and Communication of Feelings, and Was Held for Three Days From the 19th to the 21st of Last Month. Japanese Representatives Also Participated. What Was Discussed at the Meeting Was Purely What Was Proposed by the Philippines, and Opinions Were Exchanged With Each Other, and There Was No Motion. I (Jiang Claimed) Gave a Speech at the Meeting (Chinese Higher Education), and Mr. Liu Zhanen Gave a Speech (Chinese Education Trends). After the Meeting, I Went to Nearby Villages and Educational Conditions, and Left the Philippines by Ship Until the 4th of This Month.

▲Filipino Life Xu Jiang Talked About the Tour and Said That He Was Quite Moved by the Situation of the Rural Areas in the Philippines. The First Point Was That the Filipinos Were Blessed by Nature, and the People's Livelihood Was Not a Problem. The Products Were Rich, and Food and Fruits Were Everywhere. With a Little Effort, They Could Be Fed and Dressed. Living Is Also Simple. There Are No Beggars and Few Thieves. In This Superior Environment, Filipinos Hardly Believe That There Is a Hunger Problem in the World. China Is Difficult to Achieve Even With Large-Scale Engineering for Production. In the Philippines, I Asked Whether There Were Bandits in the Philippines, and the Filipinos Cried Ceaselessly. From This, You Can See the General Situation.

▲Unified Belief Second, Filipinos' Belief in Religion Is Almost Completely Unified. More Than 90% of People Completely Believe in Christianity. Therefore, What the Spaniards Have Given to Filipinos in the 400 Years Since They Arrived in the Philippines Is the Church. There Is a Church in Every Square Mile of the Village, and People's Houses Also Imitate the Church Format. The Unity of Their Belief Is Really Rare, Unlike China, Where People Worship Heaven and Earth, Believe in Buddha and Tao, and Religious Beliefs Are Absolutely Inconsistent.

▲Universal Education Third, Education in the Philippines Has Almost Become Universal. More Than Two-Thirds of the People Enter Schools. Therefore, What the Americans Have Given to Filipinos in the 35 Years Since They Ruled the Philippines Is the School. There Must Be a School in Every Village. The Equipment and Architectural Style of the Schools Follow Government Regulations and Are Completely Uniform. When the Americans First Went to the Philippines, They Brought 1,000 Elementary School Teachers From the United States. Now, Most of the Teachers in the Schools Are Filipinos. They Regard Universal Education as the Most Important Work.

▲Education Costs The Reason Why Education Is Universal in the Philippines Is That the Americans First Sorted Out Finances. The Central Government Recharges 40% for Education Expenses, the Province Recharges 40% to 60% for Education Expenses, and the Local Government (Called City) Recharges One-Third of the Total Education Expenses of the Central Government and the Province. Therefore, Education in the Philippines Is Divided Into Central Education, Provincial Education, and Municipal Education. Its Funding Is Sufficient, Which Is Unmatched by China. Secondly, the Philippines Attaches Great Importance to Rural Education. The Average Living Expenses of Rural Teachers in China Are Only 9 Yuan Per Person, Which Is Higher in Cities. In the Philippines, Talents Are Completely Distributed, Regardless of Rural or Urban Standards. Sometimes the Living Expenses of Rural Teachers Are Higher Than Those of Urban Teachers. This Is Their Characteristic, and Teachers Are Transferred to Each Other, Not Appointed by Local Teachers, So That the Language Can Be Gradually Unified, Which Can Reduce Regional Concepts. The Language Used Is Completely English, and Local Languages Are Gradually Decreasing.

▲Overseas Chinese Life There Are About 100,000 Overseas Chinese in the Philippines, Most of Whom Are Engaged in Small Commercial Businesses Such as Rice Mills, Soap, Groceries, etc. 80% of Them Are Controlled by Chinese People, but All the Living Habits of These Chinese People Have Been Assimilated. China Has Entered the Philippine Islands Since the Zhengde and Wanli Periods of the Ming Dynasty, but It Has Not Brought Other Cultures Except for Food. Moreover, the Philippines Is Not a Weak Nation and Is Quite Organized. Restrictions on Chinese Immigration, So There Are Not As Many Chinese in the Philippines As There Are in Taiwan and Other Southeast Asian Islands. In Short, the Philippines Is the Most Energetic Nation in the Ocean, and the Future Cannot Be Limited.

Points for Improving Vocational Education in Beiping City

The Ministry of Education previously dispatched Inspector Zhong Daozan to inspect the state of vocational education in Beiping City. The results of the inspection have been reported to the Ministry. The following is an excerpt from the report regarding the points for improvement in Beiping City's vocational education:

(1) There are 19 private vocational supplementary schools in the city for sewing, embroidery, knitting, typing, bookkeeping, etc., and 13 learning institutions for music, art, and hygiene. The number is not small. However, most of them have simple facilities and ineffective teaching methods. Some even have only a school sign without students or classrooms. Others have school sites that frequently move without a fixed location. Moreover, the instability of students, the lack of administrative organization, the mixing of school buildings with residential houses, and the non-compliance of course times are common problems. Strict assessment should be carried out, and subsidies and guidance should be given to those with better performance and relatively applicable facilities to improve them. Those that are poorly managed and hopeless should be ordered to suspend operations or have their registration revoked.

(2) The Municipal Senior Industrial Vocational School has achieved good results and the students' training is also good. However, the following three points should be noted: (1) The school buildings are small and the facilities are not perfect. The bureau should allocate funds to enrich the content for development. (2) Excluding drafting, the practical training hours are only 9 hours per week for lower grades and 16 hours per week for higher grades, which does not meet the regulations. Efforts should be made to increase them immediately to emphasize skills. (3) The annual product output is not large. It is impossible to assess costs with accounting. Improvements should be made quickly.

(3) The layout of the school buildings and the administrative organization of the Municipal Senior Commercial Vocational School are generally satisfactory. However, the following four points should be noted: (1) Teaching focuses on lectures. Besides typing and bookkeeping, there are few other practical exercises. Little attention is paid to commercial intelligence, economic surveys, and commodity research. (2) Commercial advertising and design are ordinary. A commodity exhibition room has not been established. (3) Experienced people should be hired for practical commercial courses. Because student employment is difficult, liaison with the business community should be made to seek service opportunities. (4) Commercial supplementary classes should not be limited to senior levels. More general commercial supplementary classes should be set up.

(4) The privately-run Zhonghua Xianqu Vocational School has not been established for long. More than 300 Xian opera performances have been produced, which is a remarkable achievement. Attention is also paid to the cleanliness and tidiness of students. The administrative organization is still organized. However, the school completely studies old operas. The teachers are opera performers, and the teaching methods are mostly outdated. Practicing martial arts often hinders the physical and mental development of young students. Attention should be paid to this. Moreover, drama is of great importance to social education. Special attention should be paid to drama reform to seek progress.

(5) The Municipal First Work-Study School enrolls fourth-grade primary school students and provides them with three years of higher primary school and vocational training. Classes are held for six hours a day with work-study. The work includes masonry, carpentry, and sewing, which is similar to a vocational supplementary school. It should be renamed the First Vocational Supplementary School to comply with regulations. Furthermore, it is said that most of the students in the school are from poor families and have few opportunities for further education. Therefore, they should be given sufficient vocational supplementary education, reduce general subjects, and increase practical work. The age limit for enrollment may be relaxed, and the length of study may be reduced appropriately. When necessary, a junior vocational course should be added to specialize in the main local handicrafts.

(6) The Municipal Huigong School is entirely elementary school in nature, except that the labor time is more than ordinary schools. Recently, the school and the Social Affairs Bureau agreed to increase the labor homework for fifth and sixth graders to 300 minutes per week, with printing and sewing. The intention is good. However, most of the students are children of workers. It seems appropriate to refer to the improvement methods of the First Work-Study School, increase vocational training, and rename it a Vocational Supplementary School. A special name should not exist.

(7) The Municipal Labor Night School and the Workers' Children's School established by the group are ordinary supplementary schools and have no labor meaning. They should live up to their names and increase vocational training, taking into account the students' family situation, and rename them all Vocational Supplementary Schools.

(8) The private Women's Western Painting School has achieved good results. It is generally satisfactory in terms of the level of higher women's art vocational education. It should be ordered to raise enough funds, increase equipment, and apply for registration in the name of a higher women's art vocational school.

(9) The five branches of the Xiangshan Ciyouyuan Private Charitable Institution are mechanics, dyeing and weaving, leather making, and carpet making. The finished products are good. In addition to factory work, there are one or two hours of classroom work per day, half of which are ordinary courses. However, the carpet department has no classroom work, and there are very few students. All work is done by workers. The administrative organization and management methods of the school are very lax. The annual business income and expenditure are almost equal. Efforts should be made to rectify it.

(10) According to the city's original plan, it is very important to increase the number of classes in the existing industrial and commercial schools and to gradually convert the Fifth Middle School into a vocational school. However, because the subsidy could not be issued according to the increased number, it was difficult to realize. Now the central subsidy has been issued according to the new amount from October of this year, with a monthly increase of 25,000 yuan. In addition to earmarking a small part for the establishment of elementary schools, the original plan to expand vocational education should be realized quickly. On the one hand, the content of each school should be enriched, and on the other hand, the number of classes should be increased. Furthermore, the Municipal Normal School currently has 12 grades, and the number of graduates each year is already too high. The number of classes should be reduced as soon as possible and transferred to vocational education or used to expand elementary schools. In this way, by shifting resources from less urgent to more urgent needs, the city's education can be expected to progress.

Private Supplementary Schools Should Issue Certificates of Achievement

▲ And Must Indicate the Period of Study and Subjects, etc.

▲ The Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to the supplementary schools yesterday to handle this matter.

The Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to the private supplementary schools in this city yesterday, which stated that Article 16 of the Regulations on Vocational Supplementary Schools stipulates that "students who have completed the period of study in a supplementary school shall be given a certificate of achievement by the school, and the certificate must indicate the period of study and the vocational subjects." All schools are required to comply with this regulation. Recently, it has been heard that each supplementary school issues graduation certificates to students who have completed their studies. The Municipal Education Bureau has returned them for correction. In the future, supplementary schools shall not submit graduation certificates to the Bureau for verification and printing. Correspondence schools and vocational training institutes shall also handle this matter in the same way.

The Secondary School Entrance Examination Ends Today

The fourth session of the secondary school student graduation examination in this city was the second day yesterday. The order in each examination hall was still good. Today is the last day. Both senior and junior high schools will take Chinese in the morning, and senior high schools will take Party Ideology and Physics in the afternoon.

The Science Society of China Plans to Organize a Large-Scale Survey Team

▲ The Survey of the Yangtze River Basin Will Take Twenty Years

▲ The Rockefeller Foundation Provides an Annual Grant of US$6,000

The Institute of Biology of the Science Society of China has been established for ten years. It has collected thousands of specimens of various natural products. Last year, it held a public exhibition of biology, which was rare in the country. Recently, it has been noted that our country is rich in natural resources. Scholars from Europe and the United States travel long distances to conduct surveys in the interior of our country every year. However, there is a lack of large-scale surveys by Chinese people. In view of this, the Society plans to organize a large-scale survey team after the completion of the biological science collection work in Hainan. The survey area will be the provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, Hunan, Sichuan, etc. in the Yangtze River Basin. The survey objects will be animals, plants, minerals, climate, forests, etc. A systematic and comprehensive investigation will be conducted. It is estimated that the survey time for each province will be two years, and the entire project will take about 20 years. In terms of funding, it is estimated that each province will cost about 20,000 yuan, and the total cost will be about 200,000 yuan. It is reported that the source of funding, in addition to the annual subsidy of 6,000 US dollars from the Rockefeller Foundation, will be raised by the Society itself. Once the funds are raised, it will organize a departure. If this move can be implemented, it will be a huge contribution to the cultural future of our country.
