Shen Bao Local Supplement Movie Special

A Brief History of Movies (3)

— Wen Ying

(3) Edison's Dream of Talking Pictures

However, the research on motion pictures by the great inventor Thomas A. Edison was not considered his main endeavor. He merely treated it as a trivial matter, thinking that with a little effort, a camera capable of continuous photography could be easily created. At that time, he was dedicated to researching electric lights. He believed that electric lights were beneficial tools for mankind. He didn't realize that when he noted the possibility of motion pictures, he was already benefiting humanity.

But things were even stranger than this. When Edison noticed motion pictures in 1886, his original intention was to create "Talking Pictures." Because at that time, he had already invented the phonograph, he wanted to attach a camera to the phonograph to simultaneously display the shapes and sounds of a person speaking or singing. He thought that such a thing would be very interesting. He didn't know that what he wanted to invent was actually the "talkie" of today. But somehow, he treated the phonograph and movies as two separate things until thirty years later, when he combined these two things to create the modern talkie.

Most likely, older people can still remember the "kinetoscope" invented by Edison or W. K. L. Dickson (who was Edison's assistant, specifically in charge of the motion picture camera). They can tell you that they put a copper coin into the hole of that clumsy machine, and they could see little people dancing or boxing inside through a peephole. This little peepshow was not taken seriously by anyone, but it was the prototype of today's movies. It was a real motion picture, the pioneer of modern movie enterprises. Soon, the lens boxes of those peepshows were enlarged, placed in individual rooms, and the people watching the peepshows no longer had to squint through a peephole. They ran into the rooms to sit and watch, and what they saw was no longer those little people. What they saw was the same size as real people, moving back and forth on the cloth screen. At that time, very few people invested in this "weird thing," only a dozen or so, but these people have now become wealthy tycoons in the film industry.

When motion pictures were first invented, anything that could move was interesting. People who made movies had not yet thought of using movies to tell stories. It wasn't until 1903 that a man named Edwin S. Porter gathered a group of second-rate actors from theaters, went to New Jersey, borrowed a string of broken-down trains from the road bureau, and made a movie with a story called "The Great Train Robbery." It was a wild comedy, a total of 740 feet long. If you want to know how long or short 740 feet is, just think that modern movies are usually 1,000 feet long per reel, and each movie usually has seven or eight reels, which only lasts for more than an hour on the screen.

After "The Great Train Robbery" came out, it caused a sensation. Motion pictures became a form of entertainment, like drama, that could be enjoyed. Of course, there were many irrationalities in that movie. The timing was inaccurate. There were no close-ups in it. There was no such thing as facial expressions. In short, the robbers were bad guys, and the heroes were good guys, but they were all walking, jumping, running, and moving back and forth incessantly.

At that time, there was no such thing as a film studio. The so-called movies were all shot outdoors. All the backgrounds were natural. The price of a movie script was about 10 to 15 yuan. If a producer was willing to spend 25 yuan, he could get a masterpiece. There were no so-called stars among the actors because the audience couldn't remember the names and faces of the actors. Their salaries ranged from about 25 yuan a week to 50 yuan. The salaries that Hollywood stars now earn were unimaginable at that time. If you knew the salaries that screenwriters earn now, you would definitely feel sorry for the writers of the past. But if you look at what they wrote, you would definitely think that they were overpaid. Benjamin Hampton, in his film history, gave us a sample of an early movie script. Here is what it is...

(A poor but proud young woman, due to the decline of her family and an elderly mother, is unable to make a living and has no choice but to go begging. A man sees her and feels sorry for her and is attracted to her beauty, and proposes to give her money. The woman is angered by his frivolousness and refuses to accept it, and plans to commit suicide. The man deeply regrets his rashness and goes to her house to apologize. He happens to see the woman committing suicide, so he saves her and leaves money for her mother and leaves. The woman wakes up and realizes that the man is sincere in his remorse and gradually develops a feeling of respect and love for him. The ending is that everyone in the play is happily united in one family, etc.).

Just a few words like this could sell a movie script for more than ten yuan, isn't that a very generous reward? But this kind of story was what our elders liked to hear the most. They were moved to tears and joy after watching that movie. They were willing to spend money to watch that kind of thing, which gave the pioneering entrepreneurs a backing, and the film industry flourished. At that time, capitalists who considered themselves farsighted were unwilling to invest in that kind of quick thing. They said that kind of thing was impermanent and would soon disappear. But the audience saw it. They liked to watch it. They crowded to watch it. Therefore, we can say that the film industry, from the beginning, belonged to the audience. (To be continued)

Movie Reviews

Review of "Million Dollar Ransom"

— Ling He

Million Dollar Ransom

Da Shanghai

To persuade the threatening and fraudulent bandits to turn over a new leaf, from the conscience is not the first time expressed in American films since "Million Dollar Ransom". This film is just retreading the same ground. However, the screenwriter who adapted the novel once again clarifies this theme in this film. His efforts to preach for the current social system cannot but show his painstaking efforts. In fact. Such artists, in addition to performing the task of preaching idealistically, have no way to cover up the chaos and unrest of the social order.

However, the screenwriter's lying ability is not very clever. For example, the main key to the plot is that the rich young man wants the great thief to kidnap himself and rewards the great thief with 20,000 yuan. In any case, it cannot be believed that this is a true expression. Since this point is so weak, the subsequent plot will naturally be incoherent.

In addition, all aspects show the vulgarity of the work. Regardless of the stylized scenery, regardless of the moving songs in the ballroom, regardless of the tranquility and natural beauty in the countryside, it still fails to achieve overall success.

As for personal acting skills, there is nothing to mention.

Audience Opinions

After Watching "The Big Road"

— Mao Di

What the directors of "The Big Road" gave us is still their consistent poetic style, anti-imperialist, and surreal.

Road construction workers will shoulder such a major responsibility for saving the nation and the country, and the wandering women and girls in the restaurant will be so alert and brave. No one dares to believe that this is a fact of the current society, as the author himself said... (In terms of consciousness, there may be some ideals!)

However, grabbing road construction workers as the protagonists of the story is not an old-fashioned theme, and the directors skillfully depict it as a relaxed, beautiful, and grand picture. The clear and concise mood makes the audience feel very interested and moved by it, such as when the road workers are tortured, when Jin Yan cuts the rope with scissors underground, this is so tense! Also, how pleasant it is to compete for a cup of tea in a small restaurant and force Li Lili to sing a new Fengyang song!

In terms of performance, everyone has an equal role to play. He can fully reveal the personality of each individual in every shot, and he created a rare follow shot, which is the close-up of everyone when Shang Guanwu set up a banquet at home.

Star talkie, directed by Zhang Shichuan, with Hu Die and Yan Gongshang in "Orchid in the Valley", will be released soon.

My Review of "The Big Road"

— Zheng Yan

After watching "The Big Road" directed by Sun Yu, I feel that the content of this film, in terms of the drama's consciousness; on the current film scene in China, can be said to be a successful work. Because the greatness and tragedy of the plot, as well as the majesty and inspiration of "The Big Road Song", awakened the audience's awareness of national consciousness. The author's surging passion and his upward spirit are truly commendable!

However, now that domestic films tend to be realistic, "The Big Road" seems to be too biased towards ideals and lacks the reality of reality. That is to say... all the characters in "The Big Road" are mostly beautified by the author's passionate ideals, rather than the facts of the current era and current society.

At the same time, the performances in the play, such as Mr. Hu (the deputy) setting up a banquet, concubines offering wine, using money to buy Jin Ge, and then privately torturing Jin Ge and others, imprisoning them in stone rooms like the former princes and ministers' private prisons, as well as Ding Xiang and Jasmine trying to rescue Jin Ge, etc.; are obviously a kind of empty ideal.

Of course, the director's sensitivity, the beauty of the shots, and the progress of the actors' expressions, such as Li Lili, are all satisfying.

Yihua Gossip

Ying Yunwei's directing work after rejoining Yihua will begin. The name of the play is "Hero of the Times", which is a full dialogue talkie.

Hu Rui's new work "Elegy of Life" has been fully completed, and Li Minghui, Wang Yin, Hu Ping, Wang Naijian, Qin Tong, etc., have all achieved extremely beautiful results.

The second talkie of Yihua Company, directed by Dan Du, starring Li Minghui and Yuan Congmei, "The Eve of the Wedding", is now two-thirds completed. At the same time, "The Fugitive", directed by Yue Feng, starring Yuan Meiyun and Wang Yin, will also be completed by the end of January.

Three songs are also inserted in "The Fugitive", one is the "Escape" song sung by Wang Yin and others, and the other two are sung by Yuan Meiyun and Ye Juanjuan respectively.

Shi Dongshan's new work "The Beginning of Man" is about to start filming, and Bu Wancang's "Triumphal Song" will also begin.

Zheng Yingshi's new work "Sleepless City" after "Flying Flower Village" has been written and will be sent to Beijing for inspection soon. It is a full dialogue talkie.

The Mandarin training class attached to Yihua Company has made great progress recently. At the same time, the Yihua authorities are also planning to establish a music class to cultivate singing talents for talkies.

Qiu Yiwei has officially joined Yihua and is in charge of sound recording matters.

Movie Novel

The Policeman Rides the Dragon (White Lies) (5)

— Xin Zhi

When Taylor Camden heard Joan blame him for avoiding her, he quickly defended himself, "No, no. At least I didn't mean to." Joan smiled again, "You saved my life, why are you treating me like this?" Joan said, hugging one of his arms tightly, and asked him to turn his head to look at the house. He saw a tall man standing on the lawn in front of the house, looking around. Joan said, "That's Assel, coming out to look for me. Let's hide quickly. There is a path in the woods over there that leads to the stone garden. The moonlight is very good tonight, let's go to the stone garden to play." So Taylor helped Joan walk on the uneven path, Joan leaned on him, giggling from time to time. At this time, Taylor Camden no longer thought about going home.

The trial of Dan Oliver's embezzlement of public funds is about to end. After a series of debates in another room, many jurors have returned to the jury box in the courtroom one by one. Everyone waited solemnly and nervously for their speeches. Sitting in the press box was Robert, a reporter for the Express, with one foot already extended outside the table and half of his butt sitting on the stool, ready to run out and call the newspaper office as soon as he heard the verdict. The defendant sat in the defendant's box, holding his head in both hands. His eyes were red and he stared blankly ahead. Sitting in the audience were Taylor Camden, Joan Mitchell, and John Mitchell himself. These people had been attending and testifying every day during the trial. At this time, the judge's gavel came down. The clerk waved to the prisoner, Oliver stood up and listened quietly to the sentence. The leader of the jury coughed, took a piece of paper and read, "As a result of our deliberations, the defendant is indeed guilty of all the charges against him." Oliver's face turned even paler when he heard this. His lips trembled, and he looked like he wanted to cry but had no tears. He suddenly stood up, waved his fist, and shouted dryly, "You have harmed me so much! If you hadn't arrested me, my money would have been paid off by now."

The courtroom was in chaos immediately. A bailiff walked up to Oliver and told him not to shout. Unexpectedly, Oliver suddenly went mad, punched the bailiff down, grabbed a gun from his belt, and aimed it at the crowd. Everyone crowded and tried to escape. Taylor Camden bravely jumped over the railing and rushed to Oliver. There was a loud bang, and Camden fell. Taking advantage of the chaos, Oliver immediately escaped out the door, pointing his gun at the crowd to prevent them from chasing him. Just as Oliver was about to leave, a woman in ragged clothes and with a haggard face suddenly squeezed to the front from the crowd, stretched out her hands, and begged Oliver not to fire. Joan only glanced at her, but her face had been deeply imprinted in her mind. In an instant, the crowd had surrounded the woman, and Joan also squeezed hard from the crowd to go to Taylor Camden's side and quickly tried to carry him to the hospital.

The days after Taylor Camden was injured were the most difficult days for Joan Mitchell. She ran to the hospital every day to see him. His life was already in great danger, hanging by a thread. Joan was also waiting for news at home at all times. When the phone rang, she was so frightened that she didn't dare to answer it. Later, the condition improved and he gradually recovered. Joan went to the hospital every day to talk to him. The degree of love between them seemed to have exceeded the level of friendship. But one thing that made Joan feel uneasy was that Camden, after being shot by Oliver, expressed sympathy for the murderer. He said, "Oliver is not a bad person. When the news came out, he tried his best to repay the embezzled funds." Joan said, "Publishing the news is the duty of the newspaper." Before she left, she deliberately angered him, "I'm going to have tea with Assel." (To be continued)

Shen Bao Local Supplement Automobile Weekly

Eve of the New York Auto Show

— Ling Yun

Not Much Change Except for the Body Style

The annual New York Auto Show in the United States is about to open on the 5th of this month again. All major American automakers will participate in the exhibition. The grand occasion is expected to be the same as in the past. Regarding the 1935 models of cars, the mechanism is roughly the same as the 1934 models. There is not much difference. However, there have been major improvements in the body style. According to the New York news on the 4th, the general situation of the products exhibited at this auto show is as follows.

Ford cars will have significant differences. All new Ford brand cars will soon be exhibited in major cities across the United States. Recently, Henry Ford declared that he expects to sell 1,000,000 Ford cars in 1935. However, many people who have seen the preview of the new car say that this estimate is still very conservative. The implication is that the sales volume will be more than this. And it is expected that the new Ford will not only be a strong enemy of various low-priced cars, but also all high-priced cars will be affected by the competition. Ford Motor Company plans to spend 415,000,000 US dollars as the cost of the annual production plan.

According to unofficial reports, the 1935 Ford V8 engine will have 100 horsepower. The brake test rate of the 1934 engine is only 85 horsepower. The 1933 V9 has 80 horsepower. Because of the increase in horsepower, the new car engine can obtain equal mechanical recovery action during acceleration and maximum speed. Another improvement of the new Ford is the increase in the power of the braking machine. It is said that the braking part of the 1935 new car has increased by 50%.

The shape of the new Ford car has increased a lot compared to the previous style. Although some people have been to their factory and seen the new car, they say that Ford's wheelbase has not increased or changed. And some people say that the new Ford has actually increased. Because of the extension of the engine on the chassis, the foot position in the new Ford car is much wider. Both drivers and passengers feel comfortable. The radiator at the front of the car is slightly thinner than before, and the tail is also smaller. But in general, this new car is no different from what has been seen in the past two years.

Other car manufacturers are very lukewarm about the reform of the front wheel suspension. However, a few companies use it as one of the characteristics of the 1935 new car. So this situation is very different from a year ago. There is certainly more than one reason why everyone is unwilling to change the front wheel suspension. But one thing that has to be noted is that no matter which car, if you want to make such a reform, it is expected to cost more than 20 US dollars. In this way, the cost increases, and the buyer has to pay more. It has an impact on sales. Therefore, some manufacturers do not want to increase the price of their products. So they came up with other methods to replace the front wheel suspension. It is said that the effect is very good, and it can also reduce a lot of car body shocks. And this method is much simpler. According to people in the automotive industry, Chevrolet and Chrysler will no longer use this style of spring in their two 1935 new cars. And other car dealers who manufacture low-priced cars will also abandon this machine. But the change is gradual, so the method is slightly different.

The two types of cars that have special modifications in terms of mechanism are Studebaker and Hudson. The new Studebaker car will use an independent front wheel spring instead of a coil spring. This spring was adopted by Chrysler and General Motors in January last year. The new Studebaker car does not have the old-fashioned pivot called "knee action" in the 1934 car. Instead of the above-mentioned device, the front wheels of the new car will be directly installed under the radiator and connected horizontally to the chassis. It is said that it is much better than the coil spring.

The original intention of the independent front wheel suspension is to increase the comfort of driving and reduce vibration and jumping. In the first few new cars that were launched in 1934, the coil spring material was too soft, so it was slippery when turning, and it was difficult to drive when the car was running too fast. Of course, in order to reduce this shortcoming, the spring can only be slightly harder. But part of the benefits obtained by abolishing the old-fashioned pivot will also be eliminated. One manufacturer wants to use automatic gear shifting on next year's new cars. Hudson's new car will use a vacuum-powered gear shift obtained from the engine. This power is the same as that of the water-wiping and automatic meshing blades that push the car window screens. Hudson will use the term "fingertip management" in its advertisements as a description. Because there is a lever near the driving rudder wheel, the size of a fountain pen, just press it with a fingertip, and the gear will change accordingly. Hudson has exclusive patent rights for this "fingertip management" before April 1, 1935. Lihe still corrects the engine's rotation according to the principle of automatic gear change. They have been using automatic gear shifting for two years.

Chrysler's (airflow) streamlined new car is similar in style to the 1934 Buick. Cadillac's LaSalle new car is also similar to the 1934 model. Walter Schmalbel and other companies' new cars will use all-metal roofs. This is also a new idea in the 1935 model. Because although the previous various cars were said to be made of all steel, the roof was always made of woven fabric to reduce the sound of vibration. Recently, due to advances in manufacturing research, it has been possible to manufacture the roof with metal.

The Past and Present of the Austin Factory

— Fu

Rapid Progress Over Thirty Years

Leading the British Automobile Industry

In 1905, the Austin factory, established in Longbridge Town, London, was merely a small workshop. It occupied an estimated area of two and a half acres, employing 270 workers. The total output of cars in the first year was only 120 vehicles. However, the present is entirely different. This great manufacturer of reliable British automobiles now occupies a total area of 220 acres, with approximately 100 acres actively utilized. The road in front of the factory extends for a mile. Compared to the cramped corner of the past, it is truly incomparable.

To maintain sufficient production, the Austin factory employs approximately 18,000 workers, producing over 60,000 cars annually. In practical terms, the current monthly delivery of various Austin models exceeds the total output of the nine years before 1914 by a significant amount. In terms of the scale and perfection of equipment, the Austin factory truly deserves to be the leader among British automobile manufacturers. All vehicles, from raw materials to the final paint finish, are processed within the single facility at Longbridge Town. This allows for strict enforcement of various quality checks and ensures full cooperation and economic convenience in management.

All forging shops, etc., transform raw materials into the various component parts of the Austin for machining. The total number of production machines specifically used for manufacturing Austin cars reaches 6,000. Compared to twenty years ago, the average value of each tool has tripled, and their total value has exceeded four million pounds to date. In the past two years, the Austin factory has expanded by approximately 330,000 square feet, at a cost of over 100,000 pounds. A recent further expansion added 127,000 square feet, costing 28,000 pounds, for the establishment of a large-scale new body assembly workshop. In two years, the factory has spent over 500,000 pounds on new buildings and machine tools, which can be considered a substantial amount. However, this significant expenditure is not wasteful, as the factory's anticipated results have all been achieved. The current weekly production of over 2,000 cars is clear evidence of its success. In 1922, it took 55 workers to produce one car per week at the factory. Today, it only takes nine workers a week to produce one car. With significant labor savings and a dramatic increase in production, the current selling price of Austin products is actually 50% lower than it was twelve years ago. For example, the 1922 Austin Seven horsepower convertible sold for 225 pounds, while today's model, which is universally acknowledged as much more advanced, sells for only 108 pounds. The difference between the past and present is significant.

If one visits the Austin factory for a tour, the meticulous management, complete equipment, and superior work capabilities will be immediately apparent, and one cannot help but be amazed. The reasons for Austin's excellence and worldwide reputation will also become clear. According to recent reports, new Austin car sales have increased by 72% compared to last year. It is easy to imagine that the 112,000 manufacturing workers directly and indirectly employed by the factory have been extremely busy recently.

Bird's-Eye View of the Austin Factory in Longbridge, England

Successful Experiment of German Steam Car

— Zhenmin

Eight-Cylinder Model Completed

The uses of steam seem to be decreasing day by day. At the same time, steam boilers, steam engines, etc., have been gradually abandoned by modern industrialists. Everyone suspects that in the near future, steam engines may disappear from the industrial world. However, reality often deviates from ideals. Due to the global economic panic and the declining production of gasoline, inexpensive and convenient steam engines and other engines are gradually being utilized by industrialists and are showing an upward trend. Recently, German automotive engineers, after numerous experiments, have proven that (steam cars) are inexpensive and highly efficient automobiles, which is a truly astonishing discovery that is sufficient to open a new record in automotive history.

The main driving force of a steam car is the combination of a (steam boiler and a (turbine)). Steam generated by the steam boiler is introduced into the (turbine). Due to the reaction force when the steam rushes out, the blades of the (turbine) are pushed, causing extremely rapid rotation. This then drives the forward gears, propelling the car forward. This system is much simpler than ordinary internal combustion engines, and there is no violent noise during start-up, which is the most valuable aspect. Currently, the German H. Ero has achieved excellent results using U-shaped (turbine) blades, as the reaction force of the steam rushing out can be increased considerably. The eight-cylinder steam car has now been completely manufactured. The cylinders are seventeen inches long and fifteen inches in diameter, with a speed range of ten to two thousand revolutions per minute. It is a fully automatic carburetor with high efficiency. The construction of recent silent aircraft is also similar.

The use of steam to drive vehicles was invented two hundred years before the birth of Jesus. The current steam car is merely an evolution of that. The difference between ordinary internal combustion engines and (turbines) is that the former produces various vibrations and noises during start-up, while the latter

Page 24

is very smooth. The advantages and disadvantages of internal combustion engine cars and steam cars are compared below.

Start-up | Internal Combustion Engine Car | Steam Car

------- | -------- | --------

Fuel | Gasoline or heavy oil | Coal and water (steam)

Driving Force | Engine | Steam boiler and (turbine)

Braking | Quick | Slightly delayed

Driving | Severe vibration and noise | Very little vibration and no noise

Speed | Cannot be too high | Can be very high

Internal Organization | Very complex | Very simple

Price per Mile | Expensive | Cheap

From the comparison above, although the braking of steam cars is slower than that of internal combustion engines, it has many advantages that internal combustion engines cannot match. In particular, its low operating cost makes it highly suitable for the needs of countries currently experiencing economic decline. We can predict that in the near future, steam cars will fill the automobile market.

The Current State of Charcoal Cars in Hunan Province (Continued)

— Yuqing

A Conversation Between Xia Zhengkun and Engineer Xiang De

(6) Asked what the maximum speed per hour of a charcoal car is on a level surface (i.e., 0% grade). When driving it myself the other day, I felt that the speed could not be arbitrarily increased after reaching a certain point. The only way to increase it was to use the momentum from downhill. Answered that this is related to the road surface. On a gravel road in Hunan, it can reach 35 miles per hour in clear weather. When driving on Jindi Road in Shanghai, it reached 45 miles per hour.

(7) Asked that on the return trip the other day, still using car number 54, carrying about ten passengers with little luggage, in heavy rain, the car struggled to climb a 5% or 4% grade even when using second gear. Is there a remedy? Answered that if only the uphill capability of the car needs to be increased, the gear ratio of the rear axle can be increased as mentioned in item 5. If it is desired to increase the horsepower of the car's engine, there are three methods: (1) increase the compression pressure in the cylinder; (2) increase the cylinder diameter; (3) install a supercharger.

(8) Asked, regarding car number 54, under what conditions of grade and grade length can third gear still be used to drive over a hill at a speed of 5 to 10 miles per hour. Answered that there is no precise test report on this. Regarding the number 54 coal car, when driving from Xia Sheshi to Changsha in clear weather, except for Wulipo (about 8% grade, nine li from Xiangtan Station), second gear was used. All other grades were managed using only third gear, without using any gasoline.

(9) Asked approximately how many pounds a coal car is heavier than a gasoline car under the same conditions, and how much the charcoal weighs. Answered that this is related to the structure of the coal gas generator. If only lightness is desired, a 1/16-inch steel plate can be used to make a generator with a diameter of 16 inches and a height of 14 inches, which can also drive the car. Its total weight is only 60 pounds, but it can only travel ten li before needing to add charcoal and is easily damaged. It can only be used for testing. Regarding the Xuanzi number 54 coal gas car, it weighs approximately 300 pounds, with the charcoal weighing approximately 50 pounds.

(10) Asked whether a coal car can be overloaded. Answered that it can be slightly overloaded, but the exact figure has not been tested. In general, all internal combustion engines cannot be overloaded too much.

(11) Asked how much money a coal car saves under the same environment and conditions. Please describe this in detail based on the results of actual field tests. Answered that the Xuanzi number 53 is a gasoline car, and number 54 is a coal car. The license plate numbers, tonnage, and age of the two cars are the same. The routes they travel are also the same. Based on the statistical comparison of the performance of the two cars over the past two months (i.e., January and February), the coal car saves approximately 17.7 yuan for every thousand li (each li is 180 zhang according to the Ministry of Works) traveled compared to the gasoline car.

(12) Asked what aspects are being focused on in the improvement of coal cars. Answered that the points being paid attention to for the time being are three: (1) increasing the horsepower of the engine; (2) reducing the need for cleaning after long-term operation; (3) making the cleaning work easier.

(13) Asked that the Changheng section of the road is not very flat, why are coal cars only seen on that section and not used on other routes. Answered that the Hunan Provincial Government has designated the Changheng section as a trial route for coal cars, so it has not yet been extended to other routes.

(14) Asked how much the Hunan Province has spent on coal gas car testing, employee salaries, purchases, and other expenses. Answered that I am only responsible for the technical aspects of the coal gas car problem. I am not aware of the details regarding the economic aspects, but the expenses are not very high. If employees are included, there were only two assistants during the testing in previous years. The purchases were also not very extensive, including only one gas analyzer, one solid fuel analyzer, and one pyrometer.

(15) Asked how many coal gas generator manufacturers there are in China, where they are located, how many places coal gas cars are used, and their regions. Answered that there are currently only two coal gas generator manufacturers in China: the China Coal Gas Car Manufacturing Company in Shanghai and the China Coal Gas Engine Manufacturing Plant in Hankou. Coal gas cars have been seen in Shanghai, Zhejiang, Hubei, Hunan, Guangxi, Shaanxi, Shanxi, Yunnan, Anhui, and other places, but the numbers vary. Last year, the two companies sold a total of approximately 100 sets of coal gas generators.

(16) Please teach me your opinion on coal gas cars. Answered that coal gas cars are indeed the only economical means of transportation in our country. Based on the results of the tests, every ten pounds of charcoal can offset the consumption of one gallon of gasoline in a gasoline car or five pounds of diesel in a diesel car. It is necessary to actively adopt them for national defense and national economic reasons. Although its structure is not yet perfect, from the standpoint of us technicians, we should strive to improve it, and not like merchants buying goods, discard it when they are not satisfied with the goods. In terms of technology, in addition to improving the materials used for construction and application, such as using refractory steel plates for the generator, the only important point is to increase the horsepower of the engine. The so-called coal gas cars are based on the use of gasoline as fuel. Although we can勉强 (miǎnqiǎng - force) change to coal gas, there are still many inconsistencies. Therefore, I believe that if we want to improve coal gas cars, the research work in the future will not be on the generator but on the engine. The compression pressure, ignition timing, cylinder diameter, valve diameter, gas duct speed, and valve opening time of an engine using coal gas are all different from those using gasoline. If we can build a special engine suitable for coal gas and install it on an ordinary gasoline car, its effect will undoubtedly be better than using the original gasoline engine. Also, scholars in the country have proposed compressing coal gas into cylinders and carrying them on the car for use, which is also a good method. However, the composition of the coal gas used should be different from what is currently used. The coal gas currently used contains more than 50% nitrogen, which is a non-combustible substance. If it is compressed together, it is not very economical. However, both of these research projects are relatively large. Hunan's financial resources are limited and it is not easy to proceed at present. I have also heard that some people in the country oppose coal gas cars and the use of charcoal as fuel, saying that our country's forests are limited and will not be able to withstand deforestation. This point seems to be unfounded. Demand can stimulate production. If the sales volume of charcoal increases, it will not only not damage the forests, but it can also promote the cultivation of forests in rural areas. Furthermore, if charcoal is not used as fuel, then coal should be used. Regardless of the difficulties that may arise when using coal, which are even more numerous and difficult to solve than using charcoal, even in terms of the amount of supply, although the reserves of coal and oil are rich, they are limited. Eventually, they will be exhausted. Charcoal, on the other hand, can be produced for as long as the sun exists.

New Materials for Building Automobile Roads

— Qin

North American road construction engineer Mr. Du Kai'er wrote an article in the New York Times discussing road construction for automobile driving. He said that in the past twelve years, the United States has spent $15,000,000,000 to build automobile highways that crisscross the country. However, in terms of today's widespread use of automobiles, the existing automobile roads are only one-tenth of what is needed. Nine-tenths still need to be built. However, the funds being planned by the US government for automobile road construction today are $400,000,000, which is obviously insufficient. To find a way to remedy this, the only option is to improve road construction engineering and adopt economical and appropriate raw materials for application.

The construction of automobile roads requires solid raw materials and a road surface that is suitable for ideal automobile roads, smooth, dust-free, waterproof, strong, and economical. All of these aspects must be considered and decided one by one. Today's automobile road construction still uses raw materials from the past. Road construction has only been improved since the historical advent of horse-drawn carriages. In the past, there was no need to pay attention to roads because there were no vehicles traveling on them. The discovery of horse-drawn carriages created a demand for a solid roadbed, marking the beginning of the development of roads. However, the weight and speed of horse-drawn carriages are far less than those of automobiles, so road construction does not need to be as solid as it is today. Automobiles weigh several times more than horse-drawn carriages, and their speed is also far greater. The roads built in the past are not suitable for today, which is very clear. Therefore, the raw materials used for road construction in the past are also not very suitable for today's road construction. So, when discussing the construction of automobile roads today, new construction materials are needed.

Cement roads are certainly outstanding among roads. The engineering department of Pittsburgh University researches road engineering and uses a special type of cement as a raw material for road construction. Several places in Pittsburgh are almost entirely built of cement. However, in general road construction, the middle is necessarily thicker than the two sides, while in cement roads, the thickness of the two sides must be higher than the middle, which is an imbalance. Moreover, cement is too solid and is not a good road surface. Therefore, few cement roads are being built today. However, cement is very suitable for the roadbed of the lower layer of roads because of its exceptional strength. Today's good roads almost all use cement as the roadbed, which is the most appropriate choice for roads. Because it is solid, even heavy vehicles will not damage it.

Recently, American road construction has made many new discoveries regarding roadbeds. Using loose sand as a roadbed can balance the road and is very economical, but it cannot withstand heavy-duty trucks. Due to this shortcoming, it cannot be considered a good choice. Using crushed stone as a roadbed is very economical but cannot balance the road, so it is also not a good strategy. Some have used carbonaceous materials and cotton cloth, but none are perfect. Therefore, other than mud, only large blocks of stone can achieve the same appropriate results for the roadbed. However, the cost of stone is twice as high as that of cement. The roadbeds of major roads in various countries using wood as a raw material are even more luxurious than stone. Although they have various advantages, they are not widely used because they are not very economical.

Today's most common roads are asphalt roads. However, asphalt roads are good in winter but not very suitable in summer. This is the drawback of asphalt roads. Therefore, road builders in Europe and America have recently been trying to create a mixture of cement, sand, and oil that can solidify into a hard block as a raw material for roads. It is currently being used in several cities. It is estimated to cost 10,000 yuan per mile, which is half the cost of asphalt roads. It is both economical and excellent, and may be the most suitable material for roads today. However, the cement must be from Portugal, and the output is not high enough to be popularized. Hopefully, there will be a large output in the future to allow for widespread application.

Germany is the best in Europe for road construction. The surface layer of its roads has a height of four inches and is very strong. Asphalt has also been gradually eliminated and replaced with other raw materials. Cement raw materials are widely used. As for the Netherlands, some roads are built from rubber, as the Netherlands produces many oak trees. Rubber roads have many benefits, although they are very expensive, they cannot be damaged. There are also rubber roads in the South Seas Islands. Vehicles traveling on them can avoid various problems. However, the production of oak trees is ultimately limited and insufficient to supply the raw materials for roads worldwide. The road construction industry is now trying to plant more oak trees.
